Fourth National Affairs Meeting of the Executive Yuan 61

Deliberated and decided on measures for closing accounts and collecting debts at the end of the year

Closing accounts should be at the end of the Gregorian calendar year

Repaying and collecting debts should follow the agreement

Without an agreement, payment and collection can be made at any time

The Executive Yuan held its fourth National Affairs Meeting on the 16th, attended by Sun Ke, Niu Yongjian, Wang Boqun, He Yingqin, Kong Xiangxi, and Wang Zhengting. The meeting was chaired by Sun Ke. (A) Report matters: (1) The Political Affairs Office reported that the cases handed over by the fourth plenary session of the third Executive Committee of the Kuomintang were handled by the Executive Yuan as soon as they arrived, and the original cases and the handling situation were compiled into a brief table every week for reference. The cases received from December 8th to 14th in the third week are now printed and distributed for review. (2) Work reports from various ministries, commissions, and provincial and municipal governments, totaling eleven items. (3) Minister Kong of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce telegraphed on the 15th, reporting that he had arrived at the Ministry on December 12th to assume his duties. (B) Matters for discussion: (1) It was resolved that the date for closing accounts would be at the end of the Gregorian calendar year. Repaying and collecting debts would still be handled according to the original agreement. If there was no agreement, payment and collection could be made at any time. (2) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce submitted the draft of the Organic Law of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for review and submission to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. It was resolved to be sent to the Legislative Yuan. (3) It was resolved to appoint Gong Xuesui as the Director of the Department of Construction of Jiangxi Province. (4) It was resolved to appoint Qi Zhenru as a member of the Henan Provincial Government. (5) It was resolved to appoint Chen Hui as the Principal of the Army Medical School. (6) It was resolved to dismiss Jiang Kui, the section chief of the Navigation Section of the Aviation Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Yang Jizeng and Mao Yi Ke, full-time members of the Armaments Research Committee of the Armaments Department; and Zhou Shungong, assistant member. Cha Zhenhu was appointed to fill the vacant position of section chief of the Navigation Section of the Aviation Department, and Li Shiqiong was appointed to fill the vacant position of full-time member of the Armaments Research Committee. Furthermore, Huang Guancheng, the director of the Army Hospital stationed in Shandong, was promoted to the rank of colonel. (7) It was resolved to appoint Xu Peihuang as the Director of the Bureau of Education of the Shanghai Municipal Government. (8) The Jiangxi Provincial Government reported that Tang Zongwei, the section chief of the Department of Civil Affairs of Jiangxi, had requested to resign, and requested approval, and that Liu Jingdu and Wang Zanxian had been appointed as section chiefs of the Department of Civil Affairs of Jiangxi. It was resolved to forward the report for appointment and dismissal. (9) The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission reported that Meng Yuanliang, Liu Xitong, Chen Geng, and Yang Yin had requested to resign due to various reasons, and Wang Yuguang was appointed to another position, and requested to be relieved of their original positions, and requested the appointment of Ma Ce, Huang Ben, Lian Chun, and Jiang Zhiyu as section chiefs. It was resolved to forward the report for appointment and dismissal. (10) It was resolved that before Minister Liu Shangqing of the Ministry of Interior arrives, Vice Minister Zhang Wohua should be appointed to act as the minister.

Chiang to Convene Meeting at Lushan 62

Chiang's Trip to Hankou Still Undecided

Lu, Zhu, and Others Return to the Front Lines Separately

The 19th Route Army Heads to Ganzhou to Suppress Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang went to Lushan from the province on the 11th of this month for a short rest and to visit historical sites. According to news from Jiujiang, Chiang arrived in Xun on the 11th at 2 PM, resting briefly at Zhang's residence on Yima Road. He then, accompanied by Shao Lizi, Zhou Fohai, dozens of aides and guards, transferred from Jiulian Automobile Road to sedan chairs and ascended the mountain. At 4:30 PM, they safely arrived at Guling. The command headquarters was set up in the Lushan Administration Bureau, guarded by the National Government Guard Regiment and the 5th Division. The Jiujiang County Magistrate was also present on the mountain to oversee all arrangements. On the morning of the 12th, Chiang, along with Shao, Zhou, and others, visited scenic spots such as Bailudong Academy, Xiaotianchi (Small Heavenly Pond), and Huanglong Temple, lingering over the scenery, and only returned to the command headquarters in the afternoon. He also telegraphed Wu Zhihui, Chen Lifu, Ma Fuxiang, Wu Tingyang, and others to come to the mountain to discuss important political matters and actively plan ways to eliminate the communist bandits. It has been decided to convene a military conference of the three provinces for bandit suppression within the next few days. On the 13th and 14th, Wu Zhihui, Chen Lifu, Chen Bulei, Ma Fuxiang, and others arrived at Guling one after another. He Jian, the commander-in-chief of the four routes, also received a telegram summoning him to come from Hankou with Liu Wendao to Xun and then to Guling to attend the bandit suppression conference, report on the recent bandit situation in southern Hunan, and seek instructions on all matters. In addition, Wu Tingyang, the former Director of the Construction Department of Guangxi, has also arrived in Guilin, reportedly to discuss issues related to Guangxi province. There are varying rumors regarding the date of Chairman Chiang's trip to Hankou. However, when Chairman Chiang left the province for Xun the other day, he told Lu that he still needed to visit Nanchang. The command headquarters at the Provincial Library in Baihuazhou has not yet been dismantled, and Deputy Adjutant Xiong of the General Headquarters is stationed there. Perhaps Chiang will return to the province when he returns east from Hankou, but this is not certain.

After Chiang went to Lushan, Lu Diping convened all staff members at the provincial government on the 13th, exhorting them to abide by the current affairs and work diligently. At the same time, he also convened a temporary meeting of various committee members, resolving to abolish the exorbitant tax of adding one yuan and four jiao per dan of salt. As for the division commanders such as Gong Bingfan, he returned to Jishui from the province on the 13th to take over the defense area of Xu Kexiang's division. Zhang Huizan also returned to Yongfeng on the same day. Lu then led the Ninth Route Army headquarters by car on the Nanzhang Road on the morning of the 15th, departing from Zhangshu, transferring to warships to go to Ji'an, ordering all units to recapture the Donggu bandit lair at the junction of Yongfeng, Anfu, and Xingguo counties, in order to recover counties such as Yudu, Xingguo, and Ningdu, and to cooperate with the Fujian and Guangdong armies in encircling and suppressing the remnants of the communist bandits. As for Zhu Shaoliang, the commander-in-chief of the Sixth Route Army, he also led the personnel of the command camp by car on the Nanzhang Road from the province to Xincun on the 15th, and then took the dry road from Xincun to Fu, to supervise the Mao, Xu, and Tan divisions in attacking the bandits of Nanfeng, Guangchang, Ningdu, Ruijin, and Shicheng, and to clear out the communist bandits on the border of Jiangxi and Fujian, before entering Fujian. As for the Jiang and Cai divisions of the 19th Route Army, they have been stationed in Pingxiang for many days. Recently, because the Mao and Chen bandits of Suichuan and Taihe were plotting to attack Ganzhou urgently, they were ordered by Chiang to advance to reinforce Ganzhou. According to a telegram from Brigade Commander Ma of the Jin Division, Ganzhou has been turned from danger to safety. However, since the 19th Route Army left western Jiangxi, scattered bandits have taken the opportunity to operate everywhere. Fenyi was captured on the 8th, and Yichun is also in imminent danger. (15th)

He Jian and Others Go to Lushan to Attend the Meeting 63

Wang Jinyu's and Hao Mengling's Divisions Ordered to Be Transferred to Jiangxi

The First Batch of Personnel from the Command Headquarters Arrives in Hankou from Jiujiang

Hankou Correspondence: Commander-in-Chief Chiang's coming to Hankou to suppress bandits has been rumored for a long time, but the date of departure has not yet been determined. Now that Chiang is stationed in Lushan, it is said that he will stay for several days and then convene a three-province bandit suppression conference in Lushan. Military and political figures here who have been summoned to go are continuously on the way. As for the personnel of the command headquarters, they have been ordered to come to Hankou first and have completely arrived yesterday. The various situations that have been discovered are recorded below.

Lushan Military Conference: Commander-in-Chief Chiang went to Lushan on the 11th to view the snow. Lu Diping, He Chengjun, Shao Lizi, Zhou Fohai, Lin Wei, and others accompanied him. Chiang then planned to convene a conference of military and political authorities from the three provinces in Lushan to coordinate bandit suppression methods in the three provinces. He telegraphed Hankou to summon He Jian, Xu Yuanquan, Xia Douyin, Xiao Zhichu, and others to participate. He Jian arrived in Hankou from Hunan on the 12th, and on the 13th, he and the Mayor of Hankou, Liu Wendao, went by boat. Xu Yuanquan, Xiao Zhichu, Xia Douyin, and Xie Bin took the Jihe wheel on the evening of the 14th, and Zhang Yinxiang and Yue Weijun took the Dehe wheel on the evening of the 15th, to go to Xun and then to Lushan to participate. As for the division, brigade, and regimental commanders waiting for instructions, about two hundred people have reported to the camp and have been ordered to return to their original defenses. After receiving the telegram, they will come to Hankou to listen to the instructions. It is said that all the important people will arrive in Lushan completely on the 16th, and the formal meeting will open within a few days.

Command Headquarters Staff Arrives in Hankou: Although the date of Commander-in-Chief Chiang's arrival in Hankou has not been determined, he will surely come to Hankou. Whether he will go to Hunan is uncertain. The staff of the command headquarters, led by Zhan Zhenhuang, the Director of the Adjutant's Office, and Luo Junqiang, the Secretary-General of the Political Training Department, arrived in Hankou on the evening of the 14th, taking the Jiangxin and Jiangtian wheels to make arrangements first. This includes two officers and seven soldiers from the Staff Office, four officers and eight soldiers from the Adjutant's Office, three officers and eight soldiers from the Management Office, four officers and four soldiers from the Military Hospital, fourteen officers and sixteen soldiers from the Political Training Office, four officers and three soldiers from the Aviation Department, two officers and three soldiers from the Public Relations Section, three officers and five soldiers from the Documentation Section, two officers and three soldiers from the Personnel Section, five officers and five soldiers from the Accounting Section, seven officers and twenty-two soldiers from the Special Affairs Section, one officer and seven soldiers from the Internal Affairs Section, three companies of guards and a platoon of orderlies from the Guard Division, one officer and thirteen soldiers from the Horse Company, one officer and thirteen soldiers from the Messenger Platoon, thirty-six soldiers from the Transport Team, and eleven officers and nine soldiers from the Wireless Telegraphy Unit. In addition, Zhou Bogan, the Counselor, Peng Zhenhuan, the Secretary, and Cui Shulong, the Section Chief, have also arrived in Hankou. Except for the Military Medical Office, the Management Office, the Transportation Office, the Political Training Office, and the Wireless Telegraphy Team, which are stationed in the former Russian Consulate, all other offices are stationed in the Command Headquarters.

The Entire Ninth Army Transferred to Jiangxi: The Ninth Army originally consisted of two divisions, the 47th Division of Wang Jinyu and the 54th Division of Hao Mengling, stationed in the Zhengzhou and Xinzheng area. The Wuhan Command Headquarters recently received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, ordering the entire army to be transferred to Jiangxi for concentration, awaiting orders to suppress bandits. The location of Wang's Division has been designated as Pingxiang, and the location of Hao's Division has been designated as Jiujiang. The Zhengzhou garrison duties undertaken by Hao's Division will be taken over by Zhao Guantao's unit of the Sixth Division. The troops are successively moving out. The Command Headquarters has already ordered the preparation of vehicles for the large-scale troop movement, with the Hunan-Hubei Railway Bureau preparing 60 trains and the Pinghan Railway Bureau preparing 20 trains. The Construction Department has also been ordered to allocate small boats for crossing the river. The distribution was completed on the 15th. Zhang Shaoluan's 160th Brigade of Hao's Division arrived in Hankou on the 14th, led by Zhang Wowei, the Deputy Division Commander, waiting for a wheel to the east. Li Wenming's 162nd Brigade arrived on the 15th and is temporarily stationed in Liujiamiao. The 161st Brigade and the Division Headquarters were personally led by Hao Mengling and set off from Zhengzhou on the evening of the 14th, and it is estimated that they will arrive completely on the morning of the 16th. After the division is concentrated in Hankou, it will take a wheel to Xun. Wang Jinyu's 47th Division will come to Hankou after Hao's Division has completely departed, taking a train on the Hunan-Hubei Railway to Changsha, and then going to Pingxiang to take over the defense area of the 19th Route Army. As for other troops, it is said that there have also been slight adjustments.

Recent News on Bandit Suppression in Hubei Province: The military affairs of bandit suppression in Hubei Province are primarily focused on clearing the communist bandits in Huang'an. The area is located in the eastern part of Hubei, bordering Anhui, and slightly to the north is Huangpi, bordering Henan. Therefore, communist bandits appear and disappear, like chasing rats. After the fierce suppression by the Xu and Xiao divisions, Huang'an has been recaptured. The remnant bandits have fled to places such as Hekou Town and Qiliping, and are now being jointly suppressed by Xiao Zhichu's division and Zhang Yinxiang's unit, and Hekou Town and Gaoqiao River have been captured. The remnants can be cleared soon. The bandits who fled to Anhui have been blocked and attacked by the Anhui army at the request of the Command Headquarters and have also been defeated. However, there are still remnant bandits holding out in the Huangsangkou area. He Long's bandit unit, which previously fled from Public Security, Jianli, and Shishou in western Hubei and southern Hubei to the border of Hunan, has repeatedly committed crimes in Nanhua, Jin, and other counties. After being jointly blocked and suppressed by the Hunan and Sichuan armies, they were again unable to succeed and returned to the border of Hubei, directly attacking Public Security County. It is reported that the county was captured by the bandits on the 13th, and the county magistrate fled to Shashi, telegraphing the province for troops. Now Xu Yuanquan's division has left Huang'an for Hankou and, upon receiving the order from the Command Headquarters, will immediately go to western Hubei to clear out He's bandits and be responsible for suppressing the bandit lair in Honghu. Xu has already formulated a plan and, after meeting with Chiang and seeking instructions in Lushan, will return to Hankou and then go to Jingsha to engage in the suppression. (December 15th)

Fujian Province's Deployment to Block and Suppress Zhu and Peng 64

Zhu and Peng's Forces Have Fled from the Jiangxi Border into Fujian Province

Fuzhou Correspondence: Zhu De and Peng Dehuai's communist bandit forces, due to the joint suppression by the Jiangxi armies, have fled from the Jiangxi border into Fujian. Currently, Zhu's bandits have invaded western Fujian from Ningdu and Shicheng, capturing Ninghua and Changting counties. Lu Xinming and Huang Yuebo's troops stationed in the area have retreated to Qingle and Guihua. Peng's bandits have also invaded northern Fujian from Yihuang and Nancheng, capturing Guangze and Chong'an counties. Shaowu and Jianyang are in imminent danger due to the thin forces of the defense army. It is reported that Zhu and Peng's bandits plan to first contact the Red Guards of the local communists in the four counties of Longyan, Yongding, Liancheng, and Shanghang in western Fujian, and the people's associations of the local communists in the four counties of Pucheng, Zhenghe, Taining, and Jianning in northern Fujian, to open up a line between northern and western Fujian, and then occupy the counties bordering the two provinces of Fujian and Jiangxi, relying on the mountainous terrain to resist the government army. As for the Fujian Province's bandit suppression forces, Lu Xingbang's unit is currently still in the Yanping and Jianning regions. Zhang Zhen's division will depart for Nanjing and Zhangping. Liu Heding's division is still in the rear area between Shuikou and Fuzhou, far from the bandit area. The provincial government, due to receiving urgent reports from various counties and telegrams from Commander-in-Chief Chiang urging action, yesterday ordered Lu's unit to quickly advance from Yan and Jian to western Fujian at double speed, and also ordered the advance unit, Zhou Zhiqian's brigade, to take the route from Shaxian and Yong'an into Guihua and Qingle, to block the communist bandits from Ninghua and Changting. The rear unit, Lu Xingbang's brigade, will take the route from Shunchang and Jiangle to Shaowu and Jianyang, to intercept the communist bandits from Chong'an and Guangze, and also ordered them to take a defensive posture temporarily, waiting for the main force to concentrate and then encircle and suppress them. At the same time, Zhang Zhen's division was urged to clear out the local communists in the four counties of Yan, Yong, Hang, and Lian in western Fujian by the end of this month, and to recover the lost territory, in order to prevent them from becoming Zhu and Peng's internal support. Liu Heding's division will concentrate in Yanping within the 20th of this month, and then depart from Shunchang and Jiangle to Jianning and Taining, to cut off the connection between the communist bandits in northern and western Fujian. Currently, Liu Heding has ordered Liu Shangzhi's brigade, stationed in Shuikou, to proceed to Yanping first, while he will lead Chen Baitai's brigade from Fuzhou to Shuikou, advancing successively. As for the defense of the rear areas in the provincial capital and northern Fujian, the marine corps Jin Zhenzhong and Lin Bingzhou and the provincial defense army Qian Yuguang and Zhang Ziming's four brigades will jointly undertake the task. Generally, Jin and Zhang's units will be responsible for the counties under the province, and Lin and Qian's units will be responsible for the counties in northern Fujian. Jin Zhenzhong's unit has already departed from the provincial capital to Lianjiang and Luoyuan yesterday, and Zhang Ziming's unit has departed from Luoyuan to the province. Lin Bingzhou and Qian Yuguang, the two brigade commanders, have also come to the province from Gutian to discuss the supply methods and defense area allocation after departing for northern Fujian. However, during this time of large-scale troop movement, there is a great need for military expenses and bullets. The provincial government specially telegraphed the General Headquarters yesterday, requesting that the previously approved military expenses of 500,000 yuan and 300,000 rounds of bullets be sent to Fujian on a fixed date for distribution.

According to military sources, Zhu Shaoliang, the newly appointed Pacification Commissioner for the Fujian-Jiangxi border, has all the divisions of Xu Kexiang, Mao Bingwen, Zhang Zhen, and Liu Heding under his command. Currently, Zhu plans to set up a Pacification Commissioner's Office in Fuzhou, with Mao's division advancing from Fuzhou to Yihuang and Nancheng, Xu's division advancing from Jishui to Ningdu and Ruijin, Zhang's division advancing from Longyan to Liancheng and Changting, and Liu's division advancing from Yanping to Shaowu and Guangze, converging on the Fujian-Jiangxi border, to attack the Zhu and Peng communist bandits who fled from Jiangxi, so that they will be attacked from both sides and have no way to escape. He himself will advance with the army and support the bandit suppression in Fujian. (December 11th)

Sun Lianzhong Comes to Jinan from Jining 65

Negotiates Defense Affairs and Downsizing with Han Fuju

Jinan Correspondence: The 26th Route Army has been ordered to be stationed in western Shandong for nearly half a month, and the various divisions and brigades have arrived successively. Sun Lianzhong, the commander-in-chief of the route army, came to Jinan from Jining by special train at around 7:00 AM today (the 13th) to report on the relocation and discuss the downsizing issue. When the train arrived in Tai'an, the adjutant of Ma Hongkui telegraphed Jinan to report. Due to the late arrival of the telegram, Sun's special train arrived in Jinan at 3:20 PM, so no one from the military or government went to the station to welcome him. Only Cheng Jiaqi, the adjutant stationed at the station of the First Army Corps, was at the station to greet him. There were eight train carriages in total. Accompanying him were Sun's wife and Deng Yuexi, the captain of the messenger team of the General Headquarters, with more than twenty bodyguards carrying pistols. The luggage was extremely simple. I visited Sun on the special train and asked about the relocation of the unit. Sun said that Ji Zhentong's 14th Division, Gao Zhihe's Special Service Brigade, and the personnel of the General Headquarters had all arrived in Jining, and the General Headquarters had been set up there. Dong Zhentang's 13th Division arrived in Juye, Gao Shuxun's 12th Division arrived in Caozhou, Zhang Huatang's 1st Cavalry Division arrived in Dingtao, and Zhu Changde's 2nd Cavalry Division arrived in Caoxian. The defense area of the 15th Division is Juye, and only the advance unit has arrived. The army has been inspected by the Central Government, and the number of personnel is 47,000 and the number of guns is 37,000. I also asked about the mission of this trip to Jinan. Sun said that the army has been ordered to be under the command of Chairman Han and stationed in Shandong Province, so it is natural to have some contact with Chairman Han. This trip is firstly to report on the progress of the relocation and future joint defense issues, and secondly, because the army has too many personnel, it should be cut back to reduce the burden on the people now that the military affairs are over. The downsizing issue also needs to be discussed with Chairman Han. There will be no long delay on this trip, and he will return to his defense area in a few days to engage in downsizing, eliminating the weak and retaining the strong, and retraining them to become a national army. I also asked about the whereabouts of Feng Yuxiang. Sun said that he did not know the whereabouts of Mr. Feng. However, Vice Commander Zhang guaranteed that Mr. Feng would go abroad, and Mr. Feng was also very willing to go abroad. This matter is no longer a problem. Mr. Feng still has 30,000 remnants stationed in Jincheng and Quwo around Yuncheng. The Central Government has also decided on a way to deal with the remnants. After the conversation, Sun took a car to Qianfoshan to meet Han Fuju because Han was in Qianfoshan at the time. (13th)

Inauguration of the New Zhejiang Provincial Committee 66

Zhang Nanxian, the new chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and committee members Zhang Naiyan, Jiang Bocheng, etc., came to Hangzhou recently after being appointed by the National Government. Yesterday, Zhang Nanxian and Jiang Bocheng went to the Provincial Party Headquarters to meet with the executive committee members, and the talks were very harmonious. This morning (16th) at 10:00 AM, an inauguration ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Provincial Government. About seven or eight hundred staff members of various agencies participated in the ceremony. The meeting began at 10:10 AM, presided over by Zheng Wenli, the President of the Higher Court. After the ceremony, Zhang Nanxian, Jiang Bocheng, Zhou Junyan, Zhang Naiyan, Fang Ce, Ye Zhuotang, and Wang Chengying raised their right hands to take the oath. Then Cai Yuanpei, the Central Supervising Committee Member, delivered a speech, saying that in the past, Comrade Zhang Jingjiang was very clean and honest in Zhejiang, very enthusiastic in his work, and willing to take responsibility. He was especially attentive to construction, and had overall plans for railways, highways, and electrical undertakings, which were being actively carried out. Unfortunately, he was physically weak and also served as the Chairman of the Central Construction Committee, so he was unwilling to continue serving as the Chairman of Zhejiang Province. The Central Government tried to retain him without success, so they carefully selected Comrade Zhang Nanxian to lead Zhejiang. He hoped that Chairman Zhang and the committee members would first strive to make the people live and work in peace and contentment, eliminate the communist bandits in the shortest possible time, and then complete the unfinished undertakings of the previous Zhang's construction plan and create what should be created, to create a model province. Next, Zheng Wenli, the Supervising Committee Member of the Executive Yuan, delivered a speech, and Ye Suzhong, the representative of the Provincial Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, the main idea of which was the same as Cai's. Finally, Zhang delivered a reply speech. The ceremony was completed at 12:00 PM. A group photo was taken in the back garden, and then a banquet with two tables was held in the reception hall of the Secretariat, inviting Cai and Zheng and the executive committee members of the Party Headquarters. Chairman Zhang then convened the secretaries and section chiefs of the Secretariat and the Civil Affairs Department in the afternoon, instructing them to inform the various sections and shares that, except for those with special responsibilities in their duties, please focus on their work.

Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Commissioner of Jiangsu, Arrives in Zhenjiang 67

The Provincial Party and Government Agencies Hold a Banquet to Welcome Him

Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Commissioner of Jiangsu, arrived in Zhenjiang at 10:50 AM today (16th) by a special express train from Nanjing. Ye Chucang, Chen Qicai, and the leaders of the Yangzhou-Zhenjiang business community welcomed him at the station. After Zhang got off the train, he and Ye took a car to the Provincial Government. At 12:00 PM, a Western-style meal was hosted in the ordinary meeting room, and the heads of the Provincial Party Rectification Committee and the various departments and the standing committee members of the Provincial Committee Chamber of Commerce were invited to attend. During the meal, Chairman Ye delivered a welcoming speech, followed by Zhang's reply. After the meal, Zhang visited the leaders of the various departments and the Provincial Party Headquarters, the National Art Museum, and the Chamber of Commerce. At 4:00 PM, he went to the Dahua Hotel to rest. At 6:00 PM, he attended a dinner hosted by the Provincial Party Headquarters. It is reported that he will go to Yangzhou the day after tomorrow. The personnel accompanying him this time are Chen Zhuoru, the Chief of Staff, Yu Junshi, the Director, (Zhenjiang Office), Sun Sifang, the Secretary-General, Li Gongjian, the Chief of Military Law, and Wang Chunru, the Adjutant. Zhang's family also came to Zhenjiang on the same train and are all staying at the Dahua Hotel. I visited Zhang recently and had the following conversation: (Question) When will you go to Yangzhou? (Answer) In two or three days. (Question) How many troops are suppressing the bandits? (Answer) There are already 30,000 people concentrated in Qingjiang. (Question) How many divisions are there? Will more arrive? (Answer) The 32nd Division of Liang Guanying has a total of three infantry brigades. There is also Zhang Huatang's cavalry division (still stationed in Caoxian) and Zhang Zhan Kui's cavalry division (still stationed in Zhoujiakou), which have been mobilized to come to Jiangsu. In addition, there is an independent brigade (Zheng Tingzhen), including a special service regiment and a pistol regiment. (Question) Will you go to Qingjiang? (Answer) After the arrangements in Yangzhou are completed, I will go to Qingjiang. (Question) Will you personally lead the bandit suppression? (Answer) The time is pressing and cannot be delayed. If necessary, I will set off myself. (Question) Will an office be set up in Zhenjiang? (Answer) It will be set up at Taikushan. (Question) Are there any newly recruited troops in Jiangnan? (Answer) No. (Question) How will you cooperate with the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team? (Answer) It has been agreed that they can be dispatched if necessary.

Songjiang People Petition for Exemption from the Construction Bonds 68

Geng Daochong and others from Songjiang petitioned the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Provincial Government to request exemption from the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Bonds, saying: Since the disaster of 1924, Songjiang County has been severely damaged. After the establishment of the National Government, there have been repeated orders to solicit the Two-Five Treasury Bonds, the Continued Two-Five Treasury Bonds, the 18th Year Customs Tax Reorganization, and the 19th Year Customs Tax, etc., with numerous items that are overwhelming. Mortgages and loans have exhausted all resources. Fortunately, unification has been achieved, and our common people hope that Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of the People's Livelihood can be implemented. However, recently, it was read in the newspaper that the Jiangsu Provincial Government had passed the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Bonds of 7 million yuan, with the first issue of 4 million yuan, ordering all counties to actively solicit subscriptions. Songjiang County was assigned 80,000 yuan, which caused Daochong and others to be extremely shocked. Songjiang County has a small territory and has never had wealthy merchants who can control finance. The only thing the people rely on for their livelihood is the income from land production. In recent years, the income of landowners has been far less than before due to the implementation of rent reduction. In addition, tenants mistakenly believe in the fallacy that it is incompatible with the Three Principles of the People, delaying and waiting, and cunning people take the opportunity to incite and collectively resist rent. Landowners have retreated to a state of contraction and incompetence, and the rights they should enjoy have been deprived of. It is only feared that the collection agencies have not been able to understand the unlimited taking and unreported use. The state, provinces, and localities have repeatedly increased various taxes, both original and additional. Compared with the amount that should have been paid in the first year of the Republic of China, converted into silver dollars, the money has increased by three-tenths, and the rice has also increased by four-tenths. Income decreases day by day, and output increases day by day. Draining the pond to catch fish, the people are almost going to perish together. Not only that, but the various districts of Songjiang County have suffered from the strange disasters of rice borers gnawing year after year, and have also suffered the tragic disaster of robbery by bandits. Wealthy households in towns have moved away, and the savings of the small people in the villages are almost exhausted. Those who operate land are in danger of bankruptcy due to the low price of land, and those who do business find it difficult to find wealthy merchants due to the desolate market. If this environment is still considered an area of wealth and taxes, seeking without end, like adding depth to water and heat to fire, the heart of the court and the ministries of not bearing to see the suffering of others will also be unbearable to see and hear. Moreover, in terms of construction, from the 16th to the 19th year of the Republic of China, Songjiang County has added more than 100,000 yuan for construction fees attached to the grain item, and road construction fees collected on a special project basis. In addition, the two-corner-per-mu donation of the Farmers Bank is nearly 200,000 yuan, and the road construction labor expenses are several tens of thousands of yuan. The burden on the people of Songjiang is not insignificant. If it is apportioned again according to the number, how can it be tolerated? I read that Article 4 of the fifth day of the Fourth Plenary Session, regarding the construction of positive aspects, should be appropriately reduced or postponed, and the various departments should not issue bonds on the issues in charge. If the issued bonds have not been fully raised, they should be raised slowly, which has been revised and passed by the Assembly. Daochong and others believe that the resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session are welcomed by the people, and the ministries and provinces should abide by them. Moreover, at this time of people's poverty and financial exhaustion, it is especially difficult to make up for one loss by creating another. We dare to jointly and sincerely request that the difficulties of the people be considered, and that the construction bonds apportioned this time be exempted from the departments, which is the convenience of the public. Citizens of Songjiang: Geng Daochong, Cai Guangyao, Du Yan, Liu Zhang, Yuan Yuan, Qu Bingchang, Zhang Baopei, Feng Shouhu, Qian Runxiu, Xie Tong, Zhang Duanjia, Zhang Bingwei, Yu Yunding, Han Lingchao, Du Zhaolun, Zhou Dang, Fei Xilun, Zhang Kaiqi, Lei Mingyang, Tang Yan, Huang Yingkui, Tang Changnian.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 69

Oil Mill in Jinshanwei Robbed: The Tongxing Oil Mill in Jinshanwei, Punan, under the jurisdiction of the county, was suddenly attacked by 60 or 70 bandits at around 4:00 PM on the 14th. More than ten of them carried pistols and rushed in first. At that time, the oil mill workers were stopping work for dinner and were held up by the gun-wielding bandits, who fired a shot as a warning. Then, they broke into the accounting room, opened the iron box, and robbed more than 1,190 yuan in silver, more than 900 corners in small silver coins, and more than 10,000 copper coins. The bandits still wanted more and broke into the bedroom of Zhang Wenjie, the village head living next door, and robbed four gold rings and 200 yuan in cash. After the robbery, they threw away the deeds and books on the ground. At that time, two patrol boats of the Fourth Detachment of the Anti-Smuggling Team stationed at the old salt canal heard the alarm and attacked, but they were outnumbered and outgunned. One patrolman was killed and several long guns were taken away. Fortunately, the Weidongmen Defense Corps and the headquarters of the Fourth Detachment heard the report and led teams to fire and pursue the bandits in the direction north behind the town. The bandits then fled northwest with the stolen goods. Zhang Wenjie, the village head of the Youchefang Village in Jinshanwei of the 16th District, and Zhang Guoquan, the manager of the oil mill, came to Songjiang to report to the county court and request an investigation and arrest of the criminals.

Establishment of the Rice Industry Trade Association: Since the Provincial Department sent personnel to guide the County Chamber of Commerce, all industries must reorganize their trade associations. The Rice Industry Trade Association has been organized and held its inaugural meeting on the 15th. The executive committee members were elected in accordance with the regulations, with Sun Jiren and ten others as executive committee members. Zhang Jiliang, Ye Yingchun, and Sun Jiren were elected as standing committee members. The members took office on the spot.

Suzhou 70

Lake Bandits Holding Hostages, Lingering in West Mountain: The Water Police Third District reported via telephone from West Mountain at 2 PM yesterday (the 16th), stating that dozens of lake bandits, in five or six bandit boats, were holding five hostages from Tong'an Bridge, as well as multiple other hostages from other cases, and were anchored at the Three Mountains area of West Mountain, waiting for the respective families of the victims to prepare funds and come to redeem them. Furthermore, a telegram from Wu County stated that bandit gangs had been discovered in the Wu-Nong area at the border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, requesting immediate dispatch of troops to suppress them. Upon receiving the telegram, District Chief Shen ordered the Eighth Water Police Team to go to West Mountain to rescue the hostages from danger, and also ordered Fourteenth Team Leader Xu to join forces with the Guerrilla Unit to head to Wu-Nong to encircle and suppress the bandits.

Removal and Prosecution of Water Police Squad Leader Yu: An elderly woman, Qian Lu, of Zhou Sidun Village, Nanbei Bridge, was targeted for theft last month by thieves Chen Agou and Jin A Jin, who failed in their attempt to steal but strangled Qian Lu to death with a rope. The local court first apprehended Chen Agou and dealt with him according to the law. Subsequently, Jin A Jin was captured by the First Squad of the Eleventh Water Police Team stationed in Fan Huang Dai. However, A Jin managed to escape. Later, the local court sent a letter to the Water Police Third District requesting the extradition of the criminal for verification by the court. District Chief Shen, upon receiving the letter, stated that Jin A Jin had already escaped without a trace. He then ordered Eleventh Team Leader Pei to place the squad leader, Yu Hongxun, under custody. Yesterday, Yu was transferred to the local court. Prosecutor Lu opened the court for investigation and, suspecting Yu Hongxun of taking bribes to release the suspect, ordered his detention. As for the Water Police District Chief Shen, considering that Squad Leader Yu had indeed engaged in illegal and derelict behavior, he had already ordered his dismissal to await investigation and prosecution by the court according to law.

Qingpu 71

Kidnapped Child Escapes Danger: Yang Jinru, a farmer from Shanxun Village, Xiping Township, was a small-scale well-off individual. The night before, eight bandits suddenly broke into his house. They first went to the house of Yang Pingfu, who lived with him, and looted it, then went to Jinru's house and looted everything. They also kidnapped his nine-year-old grandson. Later, it was discovered that the bandits had no weapons. He gathered neighbors and tried his best to chase after them. However, due to the darkness of the night, they could not distinguish the path. The bandits, fearing capture, abandoned the child on a "duan" (structure) belonging to a certain family in Zhenghong Port. The next day, he was sent back from the "bi" (structure) above, bringing joy to the whole family.

Wuxi 72

Public Bus Runs Over an Elderly Man: A visitor, Lu Fenglin (from Zhoujia Dai outside the East Gate of Jiangyin, currently 59 years old), had been working as a hired hand at the Zhu family's residence in Zhuxiang Lane, Kaiyuan Township, in this county. At around 6 PM the day before yesterday, Fenglin went to Rongxiang Town in the township for some business. Unexpectedly, when he reached West Street, a Public Bus No. 3 came speeding along. Fenglin, being deaf and elderly, was unable to dodge in time and was knocked to the ground, suffering a head injury with brain matter splattered out. He was barely breathing. Later, Patrol Officer Kang Yongzhong of the First Police Station of the Ninth Public Security Bureau of the town took the driver of the accident-causing vehicle, Zhu Guopei, into custody. At the same time, Lu Fenglin, who was injured, was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, due to excessive blood loss, the treatment was ineffective, and he died at 2 AM yesterday morning. Subsequently, Patrol Officer Kang revoked the driver's license of the bus and, together with the driver Zhu Guopei, sent him to the Ninth Public Security Bureau for transfer to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Provincial Inspector Visits Various Schools: Chen, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, recently dispatched Provincial Inspector Xiang Juetan to various places such as Suzhou and Wuxi to inspect the conditions of various schools. After being dispatched, Mr. Xiang arrived in Wuxi from Zhenjiang by train the day before yesterday. He first went to Wan'an City, Luoshe Xizhong Rural Normal School for detailed inspection. Yesterday, he inspected public and private schools in the urban area.

County Chamber of Commerce Resolves Important Cases: The County Chamber of Commerce held its eleventh joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members yesterday, chaired by Qian Sunqing. The important cases resolved were: (1) Jiangsu Provincial Business Registration: The Provincial Government resolved to change the method. It was decided to convene a meeting of representatives of various industries on the 20th to further solicit donations. (2) How to handle the case of the Ministry of Finance sending a committee to Wuxi to investigate and propose special consumption taxes. It was decided to present opinions to both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry. (3) Case of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway convening a business meeting: It was decided to nominate Cheng Jingtang as the representative to attend and to send a letter to relevant industries to compile and submit opinions to the meeting or to report the nominated representative to the meeting.

Changshu 73

Moral Learning Society Investigated, Dragon Chair Found: On the day before yesterday (the 11th) in this county, a certain Duan claiming to be a teacher of the Moral Learning Society suddenly came and held a meeting at the Zhou God Temple in the city. The decorations in the meeting were all like the former Qing Dynasty palace, with dragon chairs, dragon flags, and Bagua signs. Over the past few days, a total of three to four hundred men and women have attended the meeting. At around 9 PM on the 14th, someone went to the county party headquarters to secretly report that the Moral Learning Society was holding a secret gathering at the Zhou God Temple late at night. The county party headquarters then joined forces with dozens of police officers from the First Garrison Station, led by Shi Minyong, the supervisory committee member of the county party headquarters, and entered through the front door. At the document office, they found countless documents and a roster of members, with a total of more than 160 people signing. There was also a roster of welcomed people, with more than 260 people signing. Some old women and laborers were left there to guard the place. Then they went to the document office and found more than 200 bookcases. The books contained words such as "Permanent Moral Peace." There was also a society fee book, stating that joining the society required paying four yuan. Supervisor Shi immediately ordered everyone not to move and sat guard there. Shen Zuxian, the Minister of Propaganda of the county party headquarters, entered through the back door and went straight to the upper floor. He saw a room in the west that seemed quite secret, with a silk curtain on the door with the words "Only I am God" written on it. Shen went to the place and met a servant who said that the room was the bedroom of Counselor Tang. He was asked to get up, and a business card was produced with the words "Tang Zhi" printed on it, with the title "Counselor of the National Government" on the right. Another person produced a card with the words "Chen Mingge" printed on it, with the title "Major General Secretary of the General Affairs Section of the National Army Reorganization Committee". As for the so-called teacher Duan, his whereabouts were unknown. Then, according to Tang and Chen, they were officials of the National Government and were familiar with Duan. They had come here for sightseeing. As for the Moral Learning Society, it was religious in nature and had no other function. At that time, Shen Shi and others believed that the society had not been registered, and the fact that it was holding a secret gathering late at night was certainly suspicious, and they had to go to the county government to handle the matter. However, Tang Chen and others refused to go. Then, Wang Kunshan, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, also rushed to the scene. As a result, they were persuaded to go to the county government to meet with County Chief Tan for further disposal. Tang Chen then agreed. At this time, the police officers of the Public Security Bureau searched everywhere. Dozens of villagers were found in the downstairs room, and some books were also found on them. They were immediately detained in the Public Security Bureau for temporary custody. Then the party officials and Director Wang, etc., accompanied Chen and Tang to the county government. First, Supervisor Shi described the search and arrest process. Then, County Chief Tan asked Tang and Chen and asked for evidence of their status as officials of the National Government. They took out the National Government access pass (with a hard seal) and symbol badges, etc. County Chief Tan said, since you have come, why didn't you ask for protection? Holding a secret gathering late at night, and asked whether they could be responsible for the Moral Learning Society. Tang Chen replied that they could only prove it, not be responsible, and also said that there were other founders in Changshu, such as Jin Yiming. That night, the two were sent back, but the police were sent to guard the front and back doors to monitor them. At the same time, a telegram was sent to the Provincial Party Consolidation Committee and the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions. The next morning, the villagers (or disciples and members) in custody were voluntarily surrendered by the founder Jin Yiming, who was willing to take responsibility alone and requested that the villagers who had been detained yesterday be released. The county government then released a group of people, and Jin Yiming was ordered to be released on bail by the Erjiapu. Only teacher Duan's whereabouts were unknown. On the same day, all the furnishings at the society site were removed. On the afternoon of the 15th, Tang and Chen sent a telegram to Beijing to prove their identity and asked Qian Changzhao (a local) to prove it from the National Government Secretariat. The People's Education Center engaged in reforming prisoners: Yao Yi, the jailer and warden of the detention center in this county, recently felt that it was urgent to find ways to reform the detainees. On the 10th, he sent a letter to Yuan Shizhong, director of the Central First People's Education Center, requesting that staff be sent to give lectures in the prison every Sunday to reform them. On the 14th, Director Yuan specially sent Gui Zhi of the Museum Department and Hua Yunsheng of the Lecture Department to give the first lecture at the East and West prisons in the afternoon.

Water Police Relocating, Residents Retaining: The Thirteenth Water Public Security Team stationed in this county is divided into three squads. Except for the Second Squad stationed in the urban area, the rest are stationed in townships and towns. The Third Squad headquarters moved from Dongtang City to Baimao Town this spring for the convenience of responding to emergencies. Because it is close to the coast, bandits are easy to come and go. It was recently heard that Dianyukou needs to dispatch two patrol boats. At the request of Dongtang City, it is proposed to move the team headquarters back to the original defense area on an appointed day. However, the residents of Baimao believe that the river defense is important and should not be allowed to go elsewhere, and they have convened a meeting and elected representatives to go to the county government and the Thirteenth Team headquarters to request a postponement of the discussion.

Jiangyin 74

Qingyang Junda Pawnshop Embezzlement Case: Custody after interrogation: Jiang Yuxian, manager of Qingyang Junda Pawnshop, and Cao Zhifu of the silver room were sued by the Sheng family represented by lawyers Zhuang Zenghu, He Shousen, and Pan Liyi to the county for embezzling more than 80,000 yuan. Jiang and Cao were detained in the case. Yesterday (the 15th) afternoon, the county interrogated. Jiang Xiangxian had previously admitted to embezzling more than 24,000 yuan. Cao claimed that although there were embezzled funds, they were not more than 50,000 yuan, and there were inconsistencies. The court ordered him to submit a statement stating the reasons. The plaintiff did not arrive today and will be interrogated again after they arrive next time. Jiang and Cao were still ordered to be guarded by bailiffs in the waiting room.

Large Quantities of Opium Destroyed in Zhutang: In September, the county government cracked a case involving a large quantity of opium in Zhutang. Opium dealers Sun Huairen and others were clearly identified and sentenced separately in accordance with the anti-opium law. All the opium seized in the two incidents was specially presented to the provincial office court, which scheduled to be burned in front of the county government gate at 2 PM yesterday (the 16th). The Department of Civil Affairs also sent Zhang, the magistrate of Zhenjiang, to appoint a representative to come to Cheng to supervise.

Department Order to Investigate Grass Camp Death Case: On October 13, Cao Yangfang, head of the fifth district security team of Shengang, reported by Detective Wu Hao that he had captured Jiang Shun, Sheng Xi Binggen and Wu Yongzhen for alleged involvement in the Xie Fulin family kidnapping. The three were taken into custody, and Jiang was shot and killed at night for attempting to escape. His father, Jiang Zian, stated that although his son had always been unruly, he only committed petty theft. The reason for this shooting was that Song Guanren, Mao Xihong and others in the village had conspired to raise hundreds of silver dollars, bribed Commander Cao, falsely accused him of being a bandit, falsely claimed that he was trying to escape, and shot him on the evening of October 17. Zhang Chunhong was unwilling to pay 30 yuan, and accused them of treating human life like grass and filed a complaint with the Department of Civil Affairs. After receiving the report, the Department of Civil Affairs ordered the Jiangyin County to investigate. County Chief Li ordered the police to summon a group of witnesses, scheduled for interrogation on the 17th. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff had fled. Jiang Yuanhang and others all arrived on schedule and denied the charges after interrogation.

Rugao 75

Li Shangwu Acts Arbitrarily Across Borders: Li Shangwu, the team leader of the Hai'an security team stationed in Ma Wanggou, Lifaq District, captured Wu Tianbao, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to avenge a grudge, and confiscated the guns of the patrolling police officers. It was recently learned that Wu was arrested and taken to the team, where he was tied up tightly and whipped arbitrarily. At the same time, sentries were placed everywhere to cut off pedestrians to prevent leakage of information. After a neighbor secretly informed the Sixth District Office, Jia, a special affairs officer of the regiment headquarters, was sent to investigate and mediate the matter slightly, and Wu was released. Unexpectedly, after Wu was released and returned to the bureau, the team leader led more than 70 armed team members to Lifaq Town, threatening Wu to hand over 59 people who had been friends with Liu and Zhao. He said that unless two people were shot or 3,000 yuan was handed over, otherwise the guarantors would be handed over one by one and shot immediately. Fortunately, Wu pleaded repeatedly to avoid the disaster. It was recently learned that Wu has also reported the bizarre incident to the County Public Security Bureau. The people in the area had planned to take action after the incident, but because the team leader was violent, their lives were in danger once they took action, so they dared to be angry but did not dare to speak out.

You Fuhong and Eight Others Arrested: Jin Chengsong, the captain of the first team of the First District Security Regiment stationed in Shihui Township, encountered eight people with suspicious behavior while patrolling the road at 4 PM the day before yesterday. Woman Accidentally Hits Platoon Leader and is Beaten Severely: The sister-in-law of Dr. Gong Qingyun of the Renning Hospital on Tianningmen Street accidentally dropped a brick inside the door on the afternoon of the 14th. Unexpectedly, a platoon leader of the 133rd Brigade was passing by with his team at that place, and the broken brick hit the platoon leader's head, knocking out three incisors, breaking his lips, and causing blood to flow like a fountain. The soldiers under his command, seeing their commander injured, entered and beat the brick-throwing woman painfully. They punched and kicked her, and her body was covered with injuries. Fortunately, the neighbors interceded for her, and Dr. Gong treated her on behalf of her family and dealt with it perfunctorily. Today (the 15th) morning, the platoon leader has already set off with the army, and Gong's wife has suffered serious injuries and it is unknown whether she can preserve her life.

Prosecutor Zhou Investigates Jailbreak Case: The Jiangdu County Court Detention Center had a jailbreak during the Mid-Autumn Festival of the lunar calendar, with 40 or 50 important unjudged prisoners escaping. Except for a dozen or so who were captured on the spot with the help of the county government, the rest have not been captured so far. The High Court believed that Chen Quan, the director of the detention center, was suspected of taking bribes, so it transferred the case to the Zhenjiang Local Court for handling. Prosecutor Zhou Erkai was assigned by the Prosecutor's Office of the court to investigate. Unexpectedly, when the court transferred Chen to Zhen, he suddenly escaped on the way, making it impossible to investigate. It was recently heard that the prosecutor, especially yesterday (the 15th), accompanied Secretary Wang Xia to Yangzhou and went to the detention center to interrogate each of the prisoners who had escaped and been recaptured, and inquired about whether the director and guards of the detention center had taken bribes when they planned to escape that day. It was also heard that the prosecutor finished the interrogation at 1 PM and then took the confession across the river. Chen, the former director of the detention center, is currently said to be in Qingdao, and a letter has been sent to the court here, stating that he will go to Zhen to surrender as soon as things are over.

Huxiaoqiao Town Narrowly Escapes Bandit Robbery: About three miles away from Huxiaoqiao, three or four bandits suddenly arrived last night (the 14th) and fired several shots, hoping to rob the town. All the residents and shops were awakened from their dreams in extreme panic, and the order was thrown into chaos. Fortunately, the patrolling team received the news and immediately imposed martial law, and sent a team to round up the bandits. The bandits, seeing the preparations, fled one after another.
