Letter 80

To the Editor: I recently read a communication from Jiangyin in your newspaper on the 15th, which stated that County Chief Li personally investigated the case of the branch bureau chief arbitrarily adjudicating a soil case. This does not conform to the facts. On the 10th of this month, when our bureau sent police to inspect the inn, we found Jiang Fuxiang, a native of Xiagang, in this county, in the Yingbin Inn, accompanied by a woman from Henan, Li, pretending to be a couple. However, the language of the two parties was incompatible. The patrol captain took the police to the bureau, and the two people's words were still inconsistent after the bureau chief's preliminary interrogation. Then, in accordance with Article 43, Item 1 of the Arrest Police Law, they were each sentenced to 15 days of detention and held in custody. Later, they were bailed out by local shops. Unexpectedly, Jiang Fuxiang was reported to the county government by someone else, claiming to be a soil dealer. Then the county chief and the chief of the Public Security Bureau personally went to Yingbin Jin to investigate and brought the persons involved to the government for interrogation by the chief of the Public Security Bureau. As for the fine imposed on Jiang Fuxiang by our bureau, it was because he violated the behavior of being untidy in his whereabouts, not because of a soil case. I am writing to ask you to check and correct the record. Cui Siping, Chief of the First Branch of the Jiangyin Public Security Bureau, December 15.

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education Orders Private Law Schools to Obtain Special Permits from the Judicial Yuan 81

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed the education bureaus of Shanghai and Beiping that the Shanghai Private China Public School, Shanghai Political Science and Law College, Shanghai Law School, Beiping China College, and Chaoyang College had all been approved for establishment after the promulgation and revision of the Regulations on the Establishment of Private Political Science and Law Schools by the Judicial Yuan, which was promulgated and revised by the National Government in April of this year. Private Yanjing University recently changed the name of the Applied Social Sciences College to the Law School and added a Department of Law. It has also been ordered to comply with the regulations and apply to the Judicial Yuan for a special permit. When applying for a special permit, in accordance with Article 2 of the regulations, the school's board of directors should submit a certificate of approval for establishment approved by the Ministry, a draft of the curriculum for law or political science, an educational resume, and an equipment plan, and submit it to the Ministry for forwarding to the Judicial Yuan for review. It is hereby ordered that the bureau instruct the schools to comply. This order.

Zhejiang Education Department Expedites Handling of Backlogged Cases in Various Departments 82

Director Chen is Currently in Ganzhou: Chen, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, went to Beijing last Saturday evening to discuss important official matters. He originally planned to stay for a few days and then return. However, due to a telegram from President Jiang of the National Government from Ganzhou, he took a plane to Jiujiang on the morning of the 12th. Chen did not telegraph the Education Department from Wuhan to instruct the departments to expedite the completion of the backlog. It is now learned that the reason for the Education Department to handle the backlog is that it is settling the handled items during the reorganization of the provincial government, and that Director Chen was transferred by the central government to be the permanent deputy minister of the Education Department, so he cleared up the backlog in advance. It is not yet known when the new director will take over.

First Day of the Jiangsu Experimental Elementary School Joint Conference 83

Held Opening Ceremony... Reports from Various Groups and Sections

The Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Elementary School Joint Conference, after a resolution by the Executive Committee to hold the fourth plenary session, held the opening ceremony at 9:00 AM on the 15th of this month at the Zhenzhong Experimental Elementary School in Bamen Lane, Zhenjiang, as well as an expanded Commemoration Week. Attendees included 35 people such as Xie Shouxian and Yu Gancheng from Zhenzhong Experimental Elementary School, and 135 people from 28 schools including Hu Shuyi and Jin Lunhai from Nanjing Girls' High School Experimental Elementary School, Wei Dunyi, Gu Pin yue, Song Huaichu, Zhou Jianxi, Ma Ketan and Ding Shuming from Nanzhong Experimental Elementary School, Gao Shijun and Huang Jianbai, Shi Renfu and Chen Bangyan from Suzhong Experimental Elementary School. The chairman was Xie Shouxian from Zhenzhong Elementary School, and the recorder was Zhang Danyuan from Zhenzhong Elementary School. (1) Opening of the meeting; (2) Singing of the Party song; (3) Paying the highest respects to the Party, the national flag, and the portrait of the Premier; (4) The chairman respectfully reading the Premier's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) The chairman reported that before the work report, he would like to say a few words. This conference is held in our school, gathering all the comrades from elementary schools in the province. This is a very rare opportunity. What is worth celebrating is that our school is scheduled to hold a welcome reception this afternoon, and take the opportunity to hold the completion ceremony of the new classrooms and the establishment ceremony of the kindergarten enclosure. Please come and give us your guidance. However, our school is short of staff and has many affairs, so we may not be able to provide adequate hospitality. We hope for your understanding.

(7) Work reports from various sections and groups:

(1) The Executive Committee Standing Committee reported that in the past year and a half, it had held five executive committee meetings, four principals' meetings, and one temporary general meeting. In terms of documents, it had submitted 21 documents to the Central University Administrative Council, 5 documents to the Education Department, 4 documents to the Provincial Government, and 2 documents to the Ministry of Education. In terms of received documents, there were 19 directives from the Central University Administrative Council, 2 directives from the Education Department, and 1 approval from the Provincial Government. As for finances, there is currently a deficit of forty to fifty yuan, not including the expenses for this conference. Therefore, please pay the outstanding membership fees as soon as possible for application.

(2) The Executive Committee Research Group reported that this group was previously responsible for the new elementary school curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education for experimental education in various schools. For detailed information, please refer to the written report to save time. (3) The Executive Committee Publicity Group reported that the affairs of this group were undertaken by our school (Nanzhong Elementary School) and Nanjing Girls' High School Elementary School as recommended by the previous conference. Now, a summary of the work over the past year is reported to the conference as follows. Regarding publicity work, there should be three aspects. One is to have permanent publicity, such as publishing publications, etc., which has been discussed with the Shanghai Commercial Press and can be said to be in order. One is temporary publicity, which has been discussed with major newspapers such as Shanghai Shenxin, asking them to assist in publicity. Another is entrusted to this group by the conference. For example, the previous conference entrusted this group to find ways to contact children's newspapers. This group has contacted the Central Daily News and the Cultural Daily News in Nanjing, which are more established, to publish children's weeklies, which have now been published. This is an overview of the work of this group over the past year.

(4) The Editorial Committee of the Regular Publication reported that the third issue of Elementary School Education was edited by our school (Shang Gong) on a rotational basis. Solicitation of manuscripts began in May of this year, but very few manuscripts have been received, so the Commercial Press cannot undertake the printing. Please contribute more manuscripts so that it can be printed within this semester.

(5) The Testing Group reported that please refer to the written report of our school (Central University Experimental School).

(6) The Local Education Guidance Group reported that the overview of the work of this group over the past year is as follows: (A) The biggest difference between the local education guidance methods promulgated by the Education Department and the previous ones is the designation of special funds and the special establishment of local education instructors. However, due to the initial management's opinion on the increase in budget, there were slight disagreements, so the implementation of each school was delayed. Some have plans, and some have not yet recommended specialists to start work. The reason why our school (Tongzhong Elementary School) cannot conduct important investigations and research is this. (B) The most difficult thing for each school in the methods promulgated by the Education Department is the inconvenience of the district routes. Regarding this level, our school still troubles the Education Department to re-divide the area according to the district routes of elementary school teachers certified by the former Central University Administrative Council. However, according to the personnel in charge of the Education Department, the districts in the Department are distributed according to the number of schools in each county to facilitate adjustment, in addition to the routes.

(7) The Teacher Training Internship Guidance Group reported that the schools in charge of this group are Nanjing Girls' High School Elementary School, Nanjing Elementary School, and Suzhou Elementary School. After contacting the three schools once, our school (Nanjing Girls' High School Elementary School) was recommended to report. (1) The importance of this group: (1) This group is the key to the connection between middle schools and elementary schools. Since the reorganization of the affiliated elementary schools of various normal schools in the province into experimental elementary schools, the relationship between the middle school normal departments and the experimental elementary schools is entirely in the teacher training internship aspect. Therefore, the teacher training internship guidance issue must be resolved definitively. (2) This group is one of the three major functions of experimental elementary schools. There are three functions of experimental elementary schools in this province, and guiding teacher training internships is one of its major functions. Therefore, there must be a precise and concrete method for teacher training internships. (2) The process of research. The three schools are described separately as follows. (1) Nanjing Elementary School's research on this issue. A kind of teacher training internship method specially compiled and printed is displayed at the venue for the conference to study. (2) Suzhou Elementary School issued a questionnaire in the last semester to investigate the internship guidance methods of each school, but only eight schools received it, so it was impossible to conduct statistical reports. (3) Nanjing Girls' High School Elementary School has compiled and printed a detailed method for this issue, the Outline for Visiting Teacher Training Internships and the Internship Curriculum Standards compiled by Hu Shuyi, which will be published by the Ministry of Education soon.

(8) The Elementary School Curriculum Research Group reported that our school (Taizhong Elementary School) believes that the transformation of the elementary school curriculum should take children's lives and social life as the goal, group activities as the means, and children's activities as the process. Therefore, we are now overturning subjects and replacing them with two types of central activities and free activities. Central activities are equivalent to the design of large units, divided into fixed and temporary types. There are eight fixed centers throughout the year, taking into account the four aspects of social science, business, recreation, and life. Temporary centers are determined by children's self-initiative. Free activities are a type of work determined by children themselves or predetermined and announced by teachers, which is different every day and every week. Children choose and recognize them themselves. Our school uses this proposition to transform the curriculum. Two of the eight fixed centers have already been implemented. Our school has put the actual activities and materials on display at the exhibition venue. The remaining six have also predetermined the materials and put them on display separately. If you want to know more details, you can refer to the printed materials and activity results distributed by our school.

Continued Records of the Annual Meeting of the National Federation of Vocational Guidance Organizations 84

The situation of the annual meeting of the All China Federation of Vocational Guidance Organizations in the morning has been recorded in the previous newspaper. Photos and lunch were taken at noon, and the meeting continued at 1:30 PM. Gao Jian Si and Jiang Wen Yu chaired the meeting. First, Mr. Xu Enzeng was invited to give a speech, and then the meeting began. First, the review directors of each group, Chen Xuanshan, Chen Yuguang, and Tian Yangyao, reported, and then the discussion began. A total of 43 motions and 6 new motions were discussed. After the discussion, a vote was held to elect executive committee members. Jinling University, Nanjing Women's Vocational School, and Nanjing Vocational Guidance Institute were responsible for counting the votes. All resolutions are detailed as follows: (1) Proposal to establish vocational guidance principles (Resolution) Passed, and the original proposers were asked to provide detailed explanations for each of the eight principles. (2) Proposal for the minimum organization of local vocational guidance centers (Resolution) Passed. (3) Proposal for standard procedures for vocational guidance implemented by vocational guidance centers (Resolution) Passed. (4) Proposal for methods for implementing vocational guidance in elementary schools (5) Proposal for methods for implementing vocational guidance in middle schools (6) Proposal for methods for implementing vocational guidance in universities (Resolution) The above three proposals were handed over to the executive committee to be combined with the proposals for schools implementing vocational guidance proposed by various institutions at this annual meeting. (7) Proposal for vocational guidance application forms (Resolution) Passed. (8) Proposal for provincial, county, and municipal education authorities to set up vocational education guidance specialists (Resolution) Retained. (9) Proposal that the Federation of Vocational Guidance Organizations should suggest to the Ministry of Education that the Ministry of Education issue an order to all provinces to establish vocational guidance centers within a time limit (Resolution) Passed according to the review results. (10) Proposal to request all provincial, municipal, and county governments and educational administrative agencies to assist vocational guidance organizations in carrying out their work to maximize efficiency (Resolution) Passed according to the review results. (11) Proposal on whether the organization and undertakings of guidance centers in various places should be unified (Resolution) Passed according to the review results. (12) Proposal on whether each vocational guidance center should invite local vocational education society comrades to be basic guidance committee members (The original proposer withdrew the proposal). (13) Proposal that vocational guidance centers in various places should attach vocational education libraries as needed (Resolution) Passed, except for Article 4 of the method. (14) Proposal to determine the minimum amount of funding for vocational guidance centers in each city and county (The original proposer withdrew the proposal). (15) Proposal that this association should publish vocational guidance publications to facilitate progress (Resolution) Handed over to the executive committee for consideration. (16) Proposal to publish reports on the implementation of various vocational schools to allow the industry to understand the actual situation of various vocational schools (Resolution) Combined with the 15th proposal for handling. (17) Proposal on whether this association should organize visiting groups (Resolution) Retained. (18) Proposal to investigate vocational facilities in various countries (Resolution) The proposal was changed to entrusting students studying in various countries to investigate vocational guidance facilities in various countries. Article 1 of the method was deleted. (19) Proposal that this Federation should make detailed statistics of the various talents registered by the "vocational guidance organizations" of each group member and disclose them to the country so that factories, companies, and groups can accurately select when they need certain talents (Resolution) Passed. The method was handed over to the executive committee to draft in detail. (20) Proposal to expand vocational guidance research and publicity (Resolution) Handed over to the executive committee for handling. (21) Requesting the Ministry of Education to issue an order to all levels of schools to vigorously implement vocational guidance. (22) Proposal that elementary schools should implement vocational guidance. (23) Proposal on how elementary schools should plan to add vocational courses (Resolution) The above three proposals were combined with the fourth, fifth, and sixth three proposals and handed over to the executive committee for deliberation. The method in the 21st proposal was revised, "to the extent of issuing an order to all levels of schools across the country to comply with," and all subsequent content was deleted. (24) Proposal to organize vocational workers' night schools to relieve the general out-of-school youth. (25) Proposal that schools at all levels should pilot the tutorial system (Resolution) The above two proposals were handed over to the executive committee for handling and passed according to the original proposal. (26) Proposal to suggest that the educational administrative agencies of various provinces and cities hold vocational guidance personnel training institutes or request universities to establish vocational guidance training classes (Resolution) Passed according to the original proposal. (27) Proposal to cultivate vocational education teachers (The original proposer withdrew the proposal). (28) Proposal to advocate the establishment of various specialized training institutes (Resolution) Combined with the 24th and 25th two proposals and handed over to the executive committee for handling according to the original review proposal. 29) Proposal on whether this association should hold vocational supplementary courses. (30) Proposal to hold vocational supplementary schools as much as possible (Resolution) The above two proposals were incorporated into the 27th proposal and handed over to the executive committee for handling. (31) Proposal on how to implement vocational guidance for workers and apprentices in factories and shops to enhance work efficiency and service interest (Resolution) Passed with modifications by the review committee. (32) Proposal to focus on vocational guidance in rural areas (Resolution) Passed with modified wording by the review committee. (33) Proposal that agricultural guidance agencies in various places set up winter farmers' entertainment or supplementary meetings (Resolution) Passed with modifications by the review committee. (34) Proposal to organize a wasteland investigation team to guide immigrants to reclaim wasteland. (35) Proposal to pilot unemployment surveys and statistics (Resolution) The above two proposals were passed with modified methods by the review committee and handed over to the executive committee for handling. (36) Proposal to suggest that the central government establish large-scale beekeeping farms to guide the beekeeping industry (Resolution) Passed with added methods by the review committee. (37) Proposal on whether this association should provide assistance when vocational guidance centers in various places entrust the search and introduction of personnel but there are no suitable talents or positions (Resolution) This proposal was already proposed at the inaugural meeting of this association, and there was a method discussed, so there is no need to discuss it again. (38) Proposal on whether guidance centers should refuse to register a person who has no expertise (Resolution) Handled according to the methods determined by the review committee. (39) Proposal that vocational schools should have practical contact with the industry (Resolution) Passed completely according to the original proposal. (40) Proposal on how to communicate between the industry and the education sector to benefit vocational education (Resolution) The review nature of this proposal is the same as the previous one, and it will be handled in conjunction with the proposal. (42) Proposal that the financial and industrial circles should mutually seek to develop new social occupations with the local vocational guidance organizations (Resolution) According to the review committee's amendment, the title is "Vocational guidance organizations should formulate scientific management methods for adoption by various industries to seek the development of new occupations." (42) Proposal that this association should formulate a pattern of vocational guidance organization badges so that vocational guidance centers can follow the standard pattern to make badges to ensure uniformity and show cooperation (Resolution) This proposal is requested to be handled by the executive committee for consideration. (43) Proposal on whether the location and time of the second annual meeting should be predetermined (Resolution) The time is mid-October of the 20th year, and the location is Hangzhou, Jinan, or Beiping, to be determined by the executive committee. The newly arrived proposals are as follows: (1) Proposal that vocational education institutions should attach vocational worker training classes to cultivate practical management talents (2) Proposal that this association should invite experts to go to senior high schools in various provinces to give vocational guidance lectures. (3) Proposal that this association should advocate that various specialized talents should strive to serve the society with their knowledge. (4) Proposal that this association should suggest that the government vigorously implement the policy of soldiers as workers and soldiers as farmers. (5) Proposal that this association should request the National Government to order the educational departments of various provinces to quickly establish rural vocational normal education institutions to train teachers to benefit guidance. (6) Requesting the central government to stipulate that public funds should be used to handle relief work for beggars and vagrants (Resolution) The above six proposals were handed over to the executive committee for deliberation. In addition to visiting various educational and industrial institutions, members attending the meeting in Beijing were invited to give lectures at various schools. Chen Xuanshan lectured on university vocational guidance at the College of Education of Central University, Pan Yangyao lectured on vocational principles and vocational guidance facilities, Liu Zhanen and Jiang Wenyu lectured on vocational guidance at Jinling University, Zheng Tonghe lectured on the essentials of education at the Orphans' School, and Pan Yangyao lectured on vocational principles and vocational preparation, and Chen Xuanshan lectured on vocational selection at the Municipal Central District Experimental Middle School. Now, members from various places have left Beijing separately. Zhang Jiyao, representative of the Shandong Education Department, and Wang Gongdu, representative of the Henan Education Department, will go to Shanghai to inspect education and visit vocational guidance organizations to prepare for starting them in their provinces.

Min Education Director Cheng Bolu Resumes Office 85

Departing from Shanghai on Friday

The education community hosted a farewell dinner last night

Cheng Bolu, member of the Fujian Provincial Government and Director of the Education Department, previously escaped from being detained by military personnel and came to Shanghai. He has now received an order from the central government to return to his original post. He plans to depart on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Huaan Wheel this Friday. Last night, Zheng Tan, Zhang Yanggao, Shao Minghe, Xu Zhengji, Lu Shaoji, Cheng Kuanzheng, Ding Chongxuan, Zhong Shijie, Zhou Shang and other gentlemen from the Shanghai education community, as well as Cheng Yunhua and Hua Er and two ladies, held a farewell dinner for Mr. Cheng at the Dengtuomo Hotel. Mrs. Cheng, Ms. Zheng, also attended. Halfway through the meal, Zheng Tan and Ms. Ye Hua gave congratulatory speeches on behalf of the hosts. Mr. Cheng replied that there were three main points for this trip to Fujian Province: (1) Respect the authority of the central government; (2) Respect the education industry; (3) Respect social beliefs. There are also three points for the hope of the education community: (1) Promote science; (2) Promote sports; (3) Promote books and writing. Following Mr. Cheng's speech, Ou Kuian, President of Datong University, Xu Juntao, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, Zheng Xigu, Lu Jinhou, Cen Youchang, Ge Gongzhen, and Lin Xilian and other gentlemen spoke, elaborating on the future of education. The party ended happily at around 10 p.m.

Page 11

Free Talk: Loyalty and Integrity

Words of Wisdom from Yiqian 93

Be forgiving in all things. This is to teach us how to treat others, not to indulge ourselves.

When forgiveness is applied to others, it can also benefit oneself. When forgiveness is demanded of others, only one's own faults are seen.

There are many remarks that can only be made for others, not used for oneself.

There are also many events that can only be used to praise others, not to demand of others.

If you are not satisfied with how others treat you, then you must be cautious in how you treat others.

Between each other, it is always good to compare one's own heart with the hearts of others, and then the mood will naturally be calm.

In dealing with others, be afraid that people will not expect extravagance from me. In expecting from others, always be wary of desires being too excessive.

All wrongdoings have a source. But to blame them for their mistakes may not necessarily prompt them to change. To investigate its source is the only way to enable people to reform themselves.

When you feel that people's hearts are different, instead of recklessly blaming them, it is better to look for the reasons for the difference.

Accept both praise and criticism with restraint. One is afraid that the criticism is not severe enough, and the other is afraid that the praise is too excessive.

Party Doctrine Speech by Ms. Ye Hua 94

Our country is like a broken boat with shattered sails. It can remain unharmed largely thanks to the Premier’s doctrine. However, before the windows and doors are complete, there is always the worry of the dangers of wind and rain. The Party Headquarters is most responsible to the Party and the country. The efforts and progress of all comrades can be said to be exhaustive. The Shanghai Party Headquarters, even amidst the year-end busyness, "held a primary school student party doctrine speech contest." It is truly a deeply considered and far-sighted plan. The fourteenth of the month was the day of the final. The venue was the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which was spacious and held about eight hundred listeners. Around the perimeter stood Girl Scouts from the Chinese Women's Physical Education School, wearing round hats and red jackets, yellow shirts and yellow pants, like the royal guards of Western countries, adding much color. I will record what I saw and heard that day on the left.

Drawing Lots Before the Premier's Portrait: A total of sixty-one people participated in the speech competition, drawn from municipal schools and registered private schools. Preliminary rounds were held in three groups starting on the tenth, producing eighteen finalists from each group, who were the speakers on that day. Before the speeches began, Comrade Zhu Jiarang gathered the speakers under the stage before the Premier's portrait to draw lots to determine the order of speeches. The lots were made of chopsticks and placed in a tube, in size, style, and color just like the efficacious lucky sticks in front of the City God in the City God Temple. As the students crowded to draw lots, Mr. Zhou from the Education Bureau whispered to Pan Gongzhan, saying, "They are drawing lots before the Premier's portrait; their fate may be foretold by this." It is a pity that the Premier has no fortune verses to calm their minds. Those who heard laughed. Even Comrades Wu Kaixian and Tao Baichuan, who usually kept their heads down and did not speak, laughed heartily.

Speaking Without Knowing How to Speak: After Chairman Tong Xingbai finished his report, Party Representative Pan Gongzhan gave a speech. Then, Mr. Zhou Shang, the representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, gave a speech. Zhou opened his speech by saying, "It is already a joke for someone who does not know how to give a speech to attend a speech meeting. It is even more absurd for someone who does not know how to give a speech to give another speech. Truly a strange tale! Fortunately, I did not come here voluntarily but was forced to come. I hope you will not view it as a joke or a strange tale. So, can the reasons for not being able to speak be heard? They are: not proficient in the national language; schools lack opportunities; society forbids speaking; the written language is 'zhi hu zhe ye' (classical Chinese particles) instead of 'de le ni wo ta' (modern Chinese pronouns); and political and legal autocracy. Even casual talk is punished, so there is no room for speeches. There are not many orators in Chinese history. Although there were persuasive speakers during the Warring States period and elegant debaters during the Six Dynasties, there were none like Cicero or Lincoln, except for our Premier. He used the power of speech to explain doctrine and awaken the masses. I deeply hope that the children will emulate the Premier and use speech as the first step in saving and building the country."

Striving and Efforts of the Three Principles of the People: When the students stepped onto the stage, they could not help but feel uneasy and cautious in their hearts. However, on the outside, they were mostly calm and composed, speaking fluent national language and flowing eloquently, leaving people deeply impressed. The reporter and his colleagues Fei Kunnian, Shi Yixuan, Guo Guangji, and Wang Jie agreed to count the number of times the words "Three Principles of the People," "striving," and "efforts" appeared in each person's speech. The speaker who mentioned "Three Principles of the People" the most said it twenty-four times, while the fewest said it three times, averaging seven times per person. The word "striving" was mentioned sixteen times at most and two times at least, averaging five times per person. "Efforts" was mentioned nineteen times at most and three times at least, averaging four times per person. Other words like "Premier," "Father of the Nation," "Mr. Sun Yat-sen," "revolution," "saving the country," and "building the country" were also common, but not as frequent or widespread as the three categories mentioned above.

Recording an Old Student's Hard Work at Chi Chih 95

Chi Chih College on Jiangwan Road in this city is a well-known private university in Shanghai. It was organized with departments of Arts, Commerce, and Law. Due to regulations from the Ministry of Education, it was renamed to its current name. Hu Puan, Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, presides over the Department of Sinology. Its achievements are particularly notable. For example, Ms. Chen Naiwen, the current professor of literature at Pei Cheng Girls' School and others, is an outstanding graduate of Chi Chih and a favorite student of Director Hu. Furthermore, the Chi Chih basketball team is also famous throughout the country. This semester, an old student, about fifty years old, is studying in the Department of Sinology. His general situation is recorded as follows:

Purpose of Studying: The old student's surname and given name are unknown. It is said that he is from Hunan Province. Because the communists were disturbing his home, he moved frequently. Before he could catch his breath, he had to move again. Helpless, the old student resolutely came to Shanghai to temporarily avoid the conflict. Later, due to the high cost of living in Shanghai, he recalled his admiration for Chi Chih in Hunan. He secretly thought that it would be better to study than to sit idle in a hostel. Therefore, he registered and was admitted to the school.

A Glimpse of Diligence and Thrift: The old student is not one who is penniless. He has some property. Usually, he wears cloth clothes and cloth shoes, still the original style of the countryside. He works and rests like other students every day. However, he is not good at sports. After class and meals, he often puts his hands behind his back and leisurely strolls around the school grounds, using this to relieve his worries. Although his beard and hair are gray, his spirit is vigorous, not inferior to the young. He listens attentively to the lectures and is determined to learn. The professors all praise him. It is said that he enrolled as a first-year student. Young people who aim high and far seem to feel ashamed when they see him.

Mutual Reflection: Chi Chih has an old student, and Zhengfeng College of Arts also has an old student. The difference is that the one at Zhengfeng only takes a course in Buddhism. This old man has no beard, but he is probably over fifty years old. Some say that he came to worship Mr. Jiang Zhuzhuang's Buddhism. His words are quite close to the truth.

Celebrating Mother's Birthday at the Brahma Palace by Sheng Ying 96

Shen Youyu, named Shishan and also known as Tuotuo, is a former teacher who is now an official and brings benefits wherever he goes. His family is known for its beautiful gardens. Due to unrest, he has taken residence in Shanghai. He calls his residence Haishu Building. He honors his mother by writing books and not asking about current affairs. Mr. Huang Zongyan wrote a postscript for the building, comparing it to Su Can's Hai Zang and Mei Sou's Hai Ri, which is truly fitting. He is skilled in poetry and prose and also loves calligraphy and painting. Last winter, for his mother's eightieth birthday, he refused gifts and, with his brother Zhiping, spent a large sum of money paving the stone road in their hometown, which the villagers appreciated. Recently, on his mother's birthday again, he specially borrowed the hall of the Brahma Palace to display eighty paintings of congratulatory themes collected over the year. He arranged an exhibition and invited famous calligraphers and painters to appreciate them. I personally attended the event and saw the walls filled with beautiful and vibrant works. The paintings were four-foot vertical scrolls, all uniformly mounted, including landscapes, flowers, figures, ladies, birds, animals, insects, orchids, and bamboo, both meticulous and freehand, all complete and exquisite. In addition to more than thirty famous artists from Shanghai, there were also works from various provinces such as Hebei, Shandong, Fujian, Guangdong, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Anhui, Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan. Within this province, the majority came from Lanling, Liangxi, and Suzhou. Works by ladies and outsiders were arranged in a separate section, truly a grand sight, opening a new era of birthday celebrations. The guests included Pan Lanshi, Wang Yiting, Shang Shengbo, Shen Xinhai, Tang Dongfu, Xie Gongzhan, Hu Tinglu, Wang Shizi, Wang Leixia, Hong Lisheng, Zheng Wuchang, Ma Mengrong, Ma Daiyun, Ma Wanli, Chen Gangshu, Xie Xianou, Wu Qinmu, Yao Mocun, Zha Yangu, Guan Futing, Ding Shaoshi, Xu Muru, Xu Zhengbai, Xu Zhongqi, Lu Danlin, Zhu Rongzhuang, Tang Linze, and Wang Geyi, among others, more than seventy people in all, gathered together, toasting and conversing. After drinking, they took up their brushes and collaborated on several paintings to commemorate the occasion. It is said that Mr. Shen is still planning to collect a hundred paintings and have them printed. This gathering not only provided the joy of friends coming together but also celebrated his mother's joy and created an example for the art world.

Dissecting the Flower Gambling and Talking About the Ice Heart 97

Everyone knows the harm of flower gambling. Those who talk about it change color in disgust, but those who are deluded by it are willing to risk their lives and property for it. It is indeed so. My friend Yichuan told me yesterday two recent anecdotes about flower gambling. Although I know that the speaker is earnest, and the listeners are indifferent, I dare not but do my best since there is an opportunity to speak. Moreover, this publication has a wide circulation and may provide a little help to those who have lost their way. These are my unwavering views.

Novel Drinking Games: Yichuan was invited to a banquet last Wednesday by his sworn brother, Mr. Henai. Halfway through the drinking, Mrs. Henai, Ms. So-and-so, brought out drinking tokens stored in a ivory tube. The tube was filled with several ivory sticks carved very exquisitely. However, the carvings were all so-called gods of flower gambling. Thus, they were randomly used. Mrs. Henai and Ms. Jinyang, who was at the same table, described the harms of flower gambling as follows.

Tragedy of Drawing Water with a Bucket: There was a certain lady who lost her mother early and had no choice but to depend on her stepmother. She was ignorant of joy and sorrow in her early years. As she grew older, she was mistreated by her stepmother. However, although the lady was young, she could perceive what her stepmother liked. If she had a dream at night or heard or saw something in the morning, she would tell her stepmother. It was often accurate. In terms of money, she was surprisingly loved as if she were her own daughter. One day, the mother dreamed of drawing water from a well. In the morning, she asked her daughter. The daughter had heard the neighbors say that anyone who could not afford to seal a package would use dreams to predict. A neighbor happened to arrive and said, "Last night I dreamed of drawing water from a well, and the bucket going up and down like an axis." The daughter said, "I believe it. The flower gambling opens three times a day. The earliest one is suspended overnight, called 'diaotong' (drawing bucket), which is the fairest and without bias. Now my mother and the neighbor have both dreamed like this. You will surely win the early round." The mother believed it but did not win. The loss was even greater. The mother was resentful. The daughter was very frightened. She went to the back garden and grabbed the bucket hanging over the well and smashed it. She said, "Since things have no spirit, why do you come into my dreams to burden me?" She threw the bucket into the well. Unexpectedly, she was so angry that she used too much force, causing the bucket to separate from the rope. She worried that her mother might need to draw water and would not be able to find the bucket, and the blame would be on her. She took off her clothes and entered the well to search for it. One slip and she could never come out again. A younger sister witnessed this and ran to tell her mother. The mother said, "She brought it on herself. She deserves to die." She retrieved the body and gave it a simple burial. This happened ten days ago, as described by Ms. Jinyang.

Must Get Longevity: In flower gambling, there is something called "bide" (must get). A village scholar was old. In the era of the imperial examination, he had been an official performer. In recent years, the trend in academia has turned to science, and the scholar has become more and more frustrated and bored. In recent years, a friend took him to a gambling den to be the record keeper (in rural gambling dens, there must be someone to keep records), and he shared some of the profits. He accumulated two hundred Buddhas (currency). Recently, he heard people talk about the magic of flower gambling and saw how people made money by interpreting dreams. He was quite moved. One night, he dreamed that the school inspector came to examine him and gave him the sentence "must get longevity." He was overjoyed when he woke up. He used a large sum of ten yuan to bet on the "must get" door. When the results were announced, he was just having dinner. With a "kang le" sound (lost), he was greatly disappointed. The rice stuck in his throat, and he was choked for a long time. He failed to get his longevity. His family wept, but it was too late. This happened within the past month, as described by Mrs. Henai.

Elegant Joking Echoes: Yichuan also said that Mrs. Henai made this drinking token fifteen years ago. At that time, her husband had a mistress. Mrs. Henai made this token to play a nighttime game. Whoever won would spend the night. If everyone won, then one husband and two wives would drink and make merry all night without sleeping. If no one won, then the husband would be banished to sleep in the outer wing. That day, the drinking game was played again. The lady was also present, and she was already past her prime. The female guests who knew about it still used it to joke with her.

Warmth on My Heart (3)(3)(6) Bao Tianxiao 98

Chapter Sixteen: Earnestly Asking for Words, Cui Xiu Visits the Teacher; Generously Discussing Military Affairs, a Female Hero is Feted in a Brothel

Anything that can make people numb is easy to become an addiction. If you can control yourself, that's fine. Otherwise, you will become obsessed, which is only natural. But the fundamental point is that if you can control yourself, you won't be intoxicated by it. Therefore, people who drink only have three or four cups at first, but later they become incapable of returning home unless they are drunk. Smokers initially only have one or two cigarettes after meals, but later they smoke one after another, smoking several cans of cigarettes a day. Opium is even more unnecessary to mention. At first, they only smoke a few puffs in a friend's opium den, feeling extremely comfortable in their chest and muscles. Later, they become drowsy in the haze of opium, leading to ruin and impoverishment. People become like ghosts, unable to control themselves. Since Zuo Shichen was infatuated with Green Seclusion, he felt lost and aimless if he didn't go to Little Flower Garden for a few days. It seemed like he had become addicted. At the end of last year, Cui Yun had remarried. It was said that her new husband was a businessman from Shanghai. In terms of status, he was far inferior to the previous comprador of the steamship company. However, he had never been married and was still young, only twenty-seven or twenty-eight years old. Zuo Shichen joked with Cui Yun, saying, "You have experience now. People say, 'Learn a lesson from suffering once.' You should investigate carefully. The hearts of people outside are very bad now. Don't have something like a friend's wife flirting with you again." Cui Yun said, "There is no such coincidence." Therefore, after Cui Yun remarried, he had one less place to go. The saying "single prostitution and double gambling" is the worst thing. What is meant by "double gambling"? Whenever someone goes to gamble alone, they lack interest and courage. If someone next to them encourages them, and they have a companion, they will immediately go. If both of them win after going, they will naturally be very happy and come again the next day. If both of them lose, they will discuss how to make a comeback. Among the two, one wins and one loses, and the loser can ask the winner for help. As for "single prostitution," it is even more objectionable. For example, if you go to a brothel together, you can only go together and leave together. All kinds of love talk and things like that are not good to be self absorbed when a friend is there, and neglect the friend. Single prostitution is going alone, called "duliao" (slipping away alone). Sometimes they even hide it from their friends and do it privately. Originally, there should be no third party between a man and a woman. If there is a friend who is annoying and sticks to them, they will feel oppressed. Zuo Shichen never went to Green Ripple at Little Flower Garden alone. It was always Long Ziyun, Lin Fanzi, or Ling Zhixiang. After dinner, they would go there to sit. Occasionally, when they were in high spirits, they would invite a few people to play small mahjong and have them prepare some dishes. The cost was not much. Later, Green Ripple suddenly installed a telephone. In the past, it was not as common for brothels to install telephones as it is now. After installing the telephone, their user name was not even listed in the telephone directory.

Local News

Outcome of the Water Rate Case 117

Taxpayers Association Holds Emergency Meeting

Water Rates Temporarily Paid According to Company Bills

Price Reduction to be Studied by Special Committee

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession, regarding the water rate increase case, based on the report of the Chinese Directors of the Municipal Council, specially convened an emergency fourth general meeting at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m. A record of the results is as follows:

Attending Representatives: Yang Guoshu, Wu Yaqin, Xu Jiqing, Wen Lanting, Lu Fengzhu, Yu Zhongxian, Zhang Rulin, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Hanliang, Zhang Yilin, Lu Feibo Hong, Cao Zhigong, Sun Jingxi, Li Bohan, Sun Dipeng, Xu Tingzuo, Hu Fengxiang, Wu Zhihao, Xu Yunan, Chen Tianyin, Yan Esheng, Qian Longzhang, Wu Yunzhai, Yu Xiji, Zhao Jinqing, Hu Xi Wu, Wang Jie'an, Xie Zhongfu, Jiang Yinan, Wang Yansong, Yuan Jinchu, Hu Mengjia, Chu Huiseng, Lin Kanghou, Zhu Peiyuan, Zhang Heng Hai, Shen Tianxin, Zhang Zilian. Present as Observers: Xu Xinliu, totaling thirty-nine people.

Report on the Process: Deputy Chairman Xu Jiqing presided, with Secretary Tao Leqin taking notes. After the customary formalities, the Chairman first reported on the process of urgently convening the representatives' meeting and invited the Chinese Directors to report on the discussions regarding the water rate case at the Municipal Council's special meeting yesterday (i.e., the day before). Director Yu Qiaqing reported, stating that in July, the water company proposed increasing the surcharge by one-quarter. The Municipal Council resolved and passed this matter at the first board meeting in August. At the time, Chinese Director Bei Huadong Songsun had resigned due to his impending departure abroad. Therefore, with only four Chinese Directors, despite their best efforts to argue against it, they were ultimately unable to reverse the decision due to a difference of one vote. Subsequently, following a request from the Real Estate Association, the Municipal Council's reconsideration on September 17th was also ineffective. Afterward, the examination of the water company's accounts revealed that the guaranteed interest rate was too high. Recently, the unfortunate incident of water shutoffs occurred. Therefore, they jointly requested the Municipal Council to convene a special meeting. During the meeting, arguments lasted for three hours. The result was that there was no way to change the 9% guaranteed interest rate, and since the price increase was already a fait accompli, suspension was difficult. Therefore, it was decided that the Public Utilities Committee would hire experts to jointly study the issue in order to reduce water prices and alleviate the burden on users. The prerequisite was to immediately restore the closed water pipes. Regarding the issue of paying water fees according to the company's bills, this Association will issue an announcement. This was the process of yesterday's Municipal Council meeting, etc. Next, Mr. Xu Xinliu provided a brief supplementary report. Subsequently, Lu Feibo Hong, Chu Huiseng, Yan Esheng, Hu Fengxiang, Wang Hanliang, Yu Xiji, Zhao Jinqing, Wu Zhihao, and others spoke and discussed measures to respond to the water rate case. He De Kui explained that if the water rate were increased by one-quarter for the three months from September to December of this year, the company's income would increase by 216,616 taels. For the entire next year, it is estimated to increase by 605,000 taels, for a total income of 2,780,000 taels. Furthermore, after auditing the accounts, it was found that the company was actually wasteful in many areas. Therefore, the Municipal Council could, according to Article 23 of the contract, review the company's accounts and supervise its expenditures at any time. Therefore, the Municipal Council's special board meeting resolved that the Public Utilities Committee should hire experts to form a special committee, which is a feasible fact, etc.

Meeting Results: It was resolved that: (1) Continuing the water supply and not shutting off the water again are prerequisites. (2) During the working period of the special committee composed of experts hired by the Municipal Council's Public Utilities Committee, water rates will temporarily be paid according to the company's bills. If the special committee believes that the price should not be increased in the future, the overpaid amount must still be deducted. (3) The working period of the special committee shall not exceed the end of December of the 20th year at the latest. (4) This resolution will be published in the newspaper to notify all users. Yan Esheng and Tao Leqin immediately drafted it on the spot, and it was passed on the spot. The meeting adjourned at 6 p.m. The announcement passed by the representatives' meeting is also recorded below.

General Assembly Notice: Regarding the announcement, this case concerns the British Shanghai Waterworks' 25.1% water rate increase. A public announcement denying it has already been issued. The company unexpectedly did not seek a legal solution and took the action of shutting off the water. All users were not subdued. Even those who paid did so under duress. This is what this Association should express admiration for. Now the Municipal Council has accommodated the opinions of our attending directors and specially convened a special meeting on December 15th, taking the price increase as a fait accompli. However, the company's internal affairs should be fundamentally studied and improved, resolving that: (1) Continuing the water supply and not shutting off the water again are prerequisites. (2) The Municipal Council's Public Utilities Committee and newly hired experts will jointly form a special committee to thoroughly study methods to reduce the company's water rates, etc. This Association convened a representatives' meeting on the 16th of this month, thoroughly discussed it, and resolved that since the Municipal Council has organized a special committee to thoroughly investigate and study various issues of the water company to determine how water prices can be reduced, during the working period of this special committee, water fees should temporarily be paid according to the company's bills. When the special committee's investigation and research results are available in the future, if it is believed that the price should not be increased, the overpaid water price will still be deducted. The period for temporarily paying according to the company's bills, that is, the working period of the special committee, shall not exceed the end of December of the 20th year at the latest, etc. This special announcement is for your information.

Gathering of Various Circles

Celebrating the National Calendar New Year 118

Preparatory Committee Established Yesterday

Various Positions Elected

Regarding the promotion of the national calendar in this city, after discussions and deliberations by various circles, methods were drafted and submitted to the party and government organs for separate handling. Yesterday afternoon, various circles gathered again on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters to discuss ways to celebrate New Year's Day. Over forty people attended, including Tong Xingbai and Yang Qingyuan from the City Party Headquarters, Jiang Yi from the Garrison Headquarters, Zheng Chengqing from the City General Chamber of Commerce, and representatives from the City Government, the two-way Party Headquarters, and the Navy Headquarters. Yang Qingyuan chaired the meeting. After the customary formalities, discussions began. (1) It was decided to establish a preparatory committee with representatives from the attending organizations as preparatory committee members. (2) Eleven groups, including the City Party Headquarters, the City Government, the Garrison Headquarters, and the City General Chamber of Commerce, were elected as standing committee members. (3) A general outline of the plan for celebrating the national calendar New Year was adopted. The meeting concluded at 5 p.m. The outline of the plan is recorded as follows: 1. The preparatory matters for the celebration of the national calendar New Year in the 20th year of the Republic of China in this city shall be handled by a preparatory committee organized by various circles in this city. 2. The preparatory committee shall be jointly organized by the City Party Headquarters in conjunction with relevant organizations or groups in this city. 3. The preparatory committee shall establish a standing committee to handle daily affairs and shall be divided into the following departments: (1) The General Affairs Department shall handle documents, accounting, general affairs, public relations, and other matters not belonging to the Compilation, Recreation, or Speech Departments. (2) The Compilation Department shall handle the compilation and printing of various celebration and publicity publications. (3) The Recreation Department shall handle various recreational activities for the celebration of the national calendar New Year. (4) The Speech Department shall handle the promotion of the national calendar and the invitation of celebrities to give speeches, etc. 4. The preparatory expenses for the celebration of the national calendar New Year are temporarily set at 2,000 yuan, to be borne jointly by the City Party Headquarters and various organizations and groups in this city. 5. The proposed celebration methods for the national calendar New Year are as follows: (A) Celebration Schedule: December 28th: 1. The preparatory committee will invite personnel with research on the national calendar to give speeches at the meeting. The topic will be: "Why Promote the National Calendar?" 2. All levels of party departments and groups in this city will organize speech teams and music parade teams to set off for publicity, post slogans, and distribute leaflets. 3. Contact various shops and groups to strike New Year drums indoors and on the streets. December 29th: 1. The preparatory committee will invite personnel with research on the national calendar to give speeches at the meeting. The topic will be "Comparison of the National Calendar and the Abolished Calendar." 2. Same as item 2 of December 28th. 3. Same as item 3 of December 28th. December 30th: 1. The preparatory committee will invite personnel with research on the national calendar to give speeches at the meeting. The topic will be "How to Promote the National Calendar?" 2. Same as item 2 of December 28th. 3. Same as item 3 of December 28th. December 31st: 1. The preparatory committee will send personnel to various important roads to post "Happy New Year." 2. The music parade teams of all levels of party departments and groups in this city will set off as a whole in the afternoon. 3. The preparatory committee will invite all circles to hold a grand dinner party at 7 p.m. on this afternoon. January 1st: 1. At 8 a.m., all circles in this city will hold a group worship ceremony. 2. At 9 a.m., the Shanghai all circles celebration of the National Calendar New Year and the memorial meeting for the Premier's assumption of the Provisional Grand President will be held. 3. Starting at 1 p.m., recreational gatherings will be held in Nanshi, Zhabei, and the central city. (It is planned to request that concession cinemas show movies). January 2nd: 1. Same as item 3 of the same day. January 15th: 1. At 5 p.m., a lantern festival will be held with the participation of the people of all circles in this city to celebrate the Lantern Festival. 2. Send a letter to the City General Chamber of Commerce and various shops, uniformly hanging lanterns. (B) Publicity Aspects: 1. All levels of party departments and groups in this city will organize speech teams and music parade teams to set off for publicity. 2. Various organizations, groups, and schools should give speeches on "The Meaning and Necessity of Promoting the National Calendar" during the Premier's Memorial Ceremony or other gatherings from December 20th to January 15th. 3. Compile and print New Year couplets to be distributed to various shops and homes for posting. 4. Compile and print "Happy New Year" slogans to be posted on various important roads. 5. Compile and print leaflets promoting the national calendar. 6. Send a letter to various newspapers to publish special issues. 7. The regularly published materials of all levels of party departments in this city will publish New Year special issues. 8. Contact airplanes to distribute small slogans. 9. Send a letter to various theaters in this city to add the words "Happy New Year" before performing operas. 6. This preparatory committee will announce its dissolution after January 16th.

Various Circles Preparing

Implementing the National Calendar for the New Year 119

Three Districts and Nine Sub-Districts Formulate Implementation Methods

Executive Committee of the Three Districts Issues Orders for Party Members to Comply

Instructions from the Party Department of the Three Districts: The Executive Committee of the Third District of this city yesterday issued an order to the party members of each district sub-department to set an example and implement the national calendar, stating, "For the purpose of compliance, it has been repeatedly seen that the National Government has clearly ordered and declared, and the Citizens' Training Council of this city has also, in conjunction with the Social Affairs Bureau, formulated implementation methods and ordered compliance. However, at the beginning of this promotion, all our comrades should set an example to provide an example. Therefore, the 56th Standing Committee of this Association decided to order all district sub-department party members to set an example and implement the national calendar, etc." In addition to informing them, they are ordered to immediately comply and instruct their subordinate party members to comply as one, to be required. This order.

Methods for Implementing the National Calendar: The nine sub-departments of the three districts in this city, in order to urge all circles to implement the national calendar, have specially drafted essential methods and distributed them in lead-printed copies to various circles, stating, "It is a well-known fact that the abolished calendar is prohibited and the national calendar is implemented. However, there are still many people who privately use the abolished calendar. This is a major obstacle to the promotion of the national calendar. From now on, everyone should be determined to declare separation from the abolished calendar and faithfully follow the national calendar. The nineteenth year is coming to an end, and the New Year of the twentieth year is coming. Getting rid of the old and establishing the new, sending off the past and welcoming the future, all plans should be made early. We have specially pointed out a few things to advise our compatriots from all walks of life, hoping that you will read them, do as you are told, and persuade relatives, friends, and neighbors to implement them together. The talk is over, please remember the following things, and do not lose this paper lightly. "Things that should be prepared for the New Year of the National Calendar" (1) Every household should quickly clean up their houses and utensils, (2) The accounts of income and expenses throughout the year should be prepared to be closed early, (3) The large and small firecrackers (i.e., paper cannons) for thanking the year and celebrating the New Year should be bought early, (4) New Year's cards and New Year's gifts should be prepared early, (5) The food and materials for thanking the year and for the New Year should be prepared in sufficient quantities as soon as possible, (6) Wash old clothes and make new clothes, and smile happily when you meet in the New Year. "Things that should be done for the New Year of the National Calendar" (1) Every household should raise the national flag, hang lanterns, and post new couplets, (2) Everyone can take a break and play games for four or three days (the first to the fourth day) (3) Invite relatives and friends to hold group worship banquets, (4) You can play New Year gongs and drums, parade with lanterns, and various other games that do not interfere with public security, (5) Worship the portraits of ancestors and hold family meetings, (6) From the New Year's Day of the 20th year, the dates of all documents, contracts, books, and letters should be recorded according to the national calendar. "Things that the industry and commerce circles should pay special attention to" (1) All kinds of bills must be sent out as soon as possible before December 31st, and all accounts must be closed on December 31st, (2) On December 31st, you can collect accounts all night with lights, (3) Year-end double pay bonuses should be handled in accordance with the national calendar, (4) All industries and businesses will be closed for four days from New Year's Day to the fourth day, and will open as usual on the fifth day, (5) If workers and shop assistants of industrial and commercial firms insist on and implement the abolition of the Lunar New Year's Eve and the beginning of the year, their wages should be doubled by the employer on a daily basis, (6) The wages of workers and shop assistants of industrial and commercial firms who insist on and implement the abolition of the Lunar New Year's Eve and the first day of the Lunar New Year can be doubled by the employer on a daily basis. "Things that all circles should pay special attention to" (1) Those who do not use the national calendar to celebrate the New Year, close accounts, and take holidays are in violation of the law, (2) If the month and day of documents, books, contracts, and correspondence are not recorded using the national calendar but are recorded using the abolished calendar, the law will not guarantee them in case of disputes, (3) Those who print, sell, and purchase abolished calendar books are in violation of the law.

Next Year

Implementation of New Tariff 120

Highest Tax Increase on Tobacco

Japan and the United States Rush to Ship Goods

The Ministry of Finance will implement a new tariff next year. The entire tariff rate has not yet been announced, but according to reliable sources, the content will include the largest increase in tobacco tax. The tariff on cigarettes and cigars, originally 40%, will now be increased to 75.5%. The next highest will be jewelry and various luxury goods, such as face powder and perfume, which will be increased to 40%. The new tariff on food will be 30%, while canned food will be 20%. Paper tax and sugar tax will increase by 2.5%. The new tax on machinery will vary, with the highest being 25%. The new tariff rate on other imported goods has not yet been heard of. It is also heard that although the US government's implementation of the new tariff on China will have some impact on its trade with China, its attitude is that it does not object as long as it treats all countries equally. However, businessmen from various countries believe that it is closely related to their import and export trade. In order to avoid paying huge taxes, they are mostly rushing to load huge amounts of goods to arrive in China within the year, which is of recordable value. The details are as follows:

Large Quantities of American Tobacco Arrive: Among the imported goods in the new tariff, if foreign tobacco is imported, the tax amount must be greater than the original amount. American tobacco leaves have been purchased the most by various factories in China. Since receiving the news last month that the new tariff rate will be announced on New Year's Day, Shanghai has telegraphed the United States to ship large quantities of tobacco leaves to Shanghai in advance. The first batch of goods rushed to be shipped, worth 600,000 yuan, was imported yesterday, and the rest are also on the way. Most of them are loaded on various ships such as Tianxiang, Prince, and Old Taigu, all departing from New York, and must arrive in Shanghai within 37 days. Most of them can arrive before December 31st. It is said that this batch of tobacco leaves is worth 5-6 million yuan.

Japanese Goods Rushed and Crowded: Because China is implementing new tariffs, various Japanese merchants in Shanghai telegraphed Yokohama and Hanshin to ship the goods they ordered to Shanghai before New Year's Day in order to avoid paying the new tariffs. In recent days, after consulting with the Japanese postal company to arrange for ships to transport them, Shanghai has 12-130,000 bags of Japanese sugar and 340,000 pieces of finished goods. There are also more than 100,000 pieces of Japanese sugar and tens of thousands of pieces of yarn and cloth to Hankou and Beiyang. The Japanese postal company in Shanghai has increased the number of ships dispatched from the first batch imported today, including Tai'an Maru, Tiancheng No. 9, Bi Jun Maru, and Tsukuba Maru, together with the original Mikasa, Kasagi, Maya, and Aso, for a total of eleven ships, all loaded within 14 days. Fearing that the capacity of the eleven ships would not be enough, three large ships from the Pacific and European lines were also assigned to transport these tax-avoiding goods to Shanghai. In the Yangtze River and Beiyang, 17 ships were dispatched by the Near Seas Company to transport them on behalf. In total, in these two weeks, there are more than 30 Japanese ships specially carrying these goods to China, totaling 300,000 pieces, with an average value of 4-5 million yuan.

Wenzhou Tax Tide Temporarily Set: The Yongjia Unified Donation Bureau changed the tax on foreign and Guangdong goods to a unified donation, with a tax increase of more than ten times, which aroused the resistance of merchants and gangs. Later, the County Party Department took the responsibility of mediation and telegraphed the ministry to ask for instructions on the method. This matter has been recorded in this newspaper. Now it is known that the Ministry of Finance has issued an approval order to Wenzhou on this case. The general idea is to implement the reduction of taxes and the increase of taxes from New Year's Day, and there will be changes to the current tax rules. The collection of unified donations for foreign and Guangdong goods in Wenzhou is determined by the ministry order, but since the gang has exhausted its difficulties, it is allowed to handle the changes. The foreign and Guangdong goods there will still be collected according to the original tax amount, but the name must be changed to a unified donation, so that the maintenance of the ministry order is maintained while the hardships of the merchants are actually understood. The merchants and gangs are very satisfied with this. Shanghai-Wenzhou foreign and Guangdong goods are now being loaded as usual.
