I hope you will convey this information, etc." The corresponding letter is a reply to hope you will check for information.

Jardine Matheson

Final Statement from Seamen 122

Company Refuses to Increase Salary

Branch Releases Declaration

The three departments of stewards, firemen and seamen serving on foreign merchant ships requested six foreign shipping companies to follow the example of Chinese ships and increase wages by six yuan per person per month. Only Taikoo Company, mediated by Yu Qiaqing, signed a wage increase contract in late November. This matter has been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. However, the British Jardine Matheson did not respond to the seamen's request, which has aroused the public anger of all the seamen of Jianghai. They are prepared to take final measures against the company and carry out a strike to promote the company's awareness. The reporter went to various parties to investigate the ins and outs of the matter in detail and recorded their declarations, etc., as follows:

Seamen's Request Process: After Taikoo agreed to increase the monthly salary of seamen on various ships by five yuan, the seamen on various Jardine Matheson ships believed that the matter was the same, and Jardine Matheson had previously declared that if Taikoo increased salaries, the company would also increase them accordingly. Unexpectedly, after Taikoo signed the contract, Jardine Matheson made no statement. The seamen sent representatives to inquire, and the company initially made excuses that the shipping industry was sluggish this year and requested a postponement. When the seamen repeatedly sent letters urging them, the company ignored them. Later, representatives from the union went to inquire, but the company did not respond sincerely and delayed until now. Another month has passed, and there has been no result. The seamen could no longer bear it and publicly agreed to deal with the company with final and decisive measures.

Petitioning for Central Assistance: Jardine Matheson has about 30 ships sailing on the Yangtze River and the Northern Seas, with more than 1,000 seamen. They are very angry about the failure to request a salary increase. Recently, the foreigners of the company have even used oppressive measures to force seamen on each ship to state that they do not want a salary increase in order to suppress the salary increase movement. The seamen have held many meetings and decided to take final steps. Therefore, the seamen's branch was requested to, based on the requests of the seamen, fully state the impact of rising living standards and the pain of oppression by imperialists, and to describe in detail the process of requesting a salary increase from Jardine Matheson and the company's conspiracy to sabotage the labor movement and refuse to increase salaries, and to request assistance from the Central Government. Now, in order to maintain their own livelihoods, the seamen have to make further statements. If there is no satisfactory reply, the seamen have to go on strike to promote the awakening of the capitalists. This petition was forwarded by the branch on behalf of the seamen's general union to the Central Government. When the Central Government's approval order arrives in Shanghai, the seamen will go on strike. It is heard that the petition can be sent out today.

Declaration Released Yesterday: The seamen's branch specially issued a declaration on this case, requesting assistance from all circles. The declaration is recorded as follows: "Material civilization and the daily decline of life are recognized by all countries. At this time, those who suffer the most are workers. The economic difficulties of workers have reached an extreme point. The trend is like this and cannot be stopped. Therefore, workers in various industries have asked capitalists to increase their salaries to help them make ends meet."

"There are countless examples. Our seamen work in the waves and serve on long journeys. They have no fixed rest and no fixed working hours. They are more arduous than other workers, but their salaries are still the same as they were more than ten years ago. In the past ten years, production has increased day by day, and prices have increased even more. In proportion, it has exceeded more than ten times. If calculated according to the salary earned, how can it be enough to support a family and sustain life? Workers on various ships have repeatedly stated their hardships and requested to negotiate a salary increase. Looking back on the past and present, the situation is true and reasonable. This association, in view of the fact that the passenger, cargo, and water feet of various companies have increased several times, while the wages of workers are still the same as before, believes that the thickness is inherently uneven and the reasons are insufficient. Therefore, it reported to the general union, dispatched personnel to cooperate, and consulted with various shipping companies. Mr. Yu Qiaqing generously supported the result. Taikoo (added four yuan from September 1st of this year, because the company had already automatically added it), China Merchants, and various Chinese shipping companies (added four yuan from August 1st of this year, and another two yuan from March 1st of the 20th year) signed contracts and added them one after another. However, Jardine Matheson has no sincerity at all. It compromises with the workers on the surface, but oppresses them in every possible way in secret, forcing the workers to say that they do not want a salary increase. At this time, how can any worker not want a salary increase? How can there be such a reason in the world? During the May 30th strike, the company arbitrarily fired workers. Those who were willing to stay generally reduced their wages. At that time, workers had to endure it for the sake of survival. It has been several years now. The company's conspiracy is clearly revealed, and it is so inhumane. This association is a seamen's group, and it was founded by the Premier himself. It bears a heavy responsibility and its duties are closely related. It should adhere to the Premier's legacy and, in addition to peace, only struggle. When it is absolutely necessary, it will lead hundreds of thousands of seamen to deal with the capitalists with the inherent power of workers. Therefore, I hereby inform all circles, declare the details, and hope to provide assistance so that our seamen can live. This is what I pray for. This declaration."

Yesterday's Report on Xiong Yang's Injuries 123

Li Dezhao Returned to Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday

Commander Xiong Inquired About the Bandit Suppression Situation

Zhang Qun Visited Yang Yesterday, Asking Him to Rest

The following is a report on the injuries of Xiong Shihui, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, and Yang Yongtai, Advisor to the General Headquarters, as of yesterday:

Xiong's Condition: He slept soundly for six hours on the night of the 15th. After waking up on the morning of the 16th, his spirits were excellent and his body felt quite comfortable. At 9:30 a.m., Dean Niu Huisheng again used X-rays to examine the fractured bone, and the connection was very good. He could urinate and defecate on his own. His diet included chicken porridge, soybean curd, vegetable soup, and juice. His temperature was 99.2 degrees, his pulse was 86, and his respiration was 20. Caring About Bandit Suppression: Xiong's secretary, Li Dezhao, went to Gan Province before Xiong to arrange everything. After hearing the news in Jiujiang that Commander Xiong was injured, he immediately went to see Chairman Jiang and reported everything. He returned to Shanghai by train from Beijing the night before and went to the orthopedic hospital yesterday morning to visit Commander Xiong and report on the bandit suppression situation in Gan Province. Commander Xiong inquired in great detail. Hearing that the government troops were arriving and the bandits were scattering, Xiong looked quite pleased. Yesterday, Central Committee member Chu Minyi, Zhang Qun, Lin Zhiyuan from the Fujian Provincial Committee, Xiao Shu, Zhu Shiming, Zhou Yongneng, and others all went to the hospital to express their condolences to Xiong.

Yang's Condition: Yang's cough has not stopped, but the blood in his sputum has gone. His joints still hurt, but he can sit up with light support. He slept very peacefully before 2:00 a.m. From 2:00 a.m. to 4:00 a.m., his cough worsened, but after 4:00 a.m. he was better again. The doctor prescribed cough medicine. His daily food intake has increased again. His temperature is 37.3 degrees Celsius and his pulse is 84.

Zhang Qun's Condolences: Yesterday, those who went to Baolong Hospital to express their condolences included Central Committee member Wu Tiecheng, Chen Guofu's representative Chen Xizeng, and Mayor Zhang. Mayor Zhang talked with Yang for a long time. Because Yang had not had an X-ray before, the extent of internal injuries was unknown, and there was concern about brain congestion and pleurisy. Now, after a Parker examination, it has been proven that there is no danger. After Yang explained this to Zhang, Zhang asked him to rest and recuperate peacefully.

This City Will Implement Standardized Weights and Measures on Schedule 124

The Municipal Government Instructed the Bureau of Social Affairs to Comply

The Municipal Government, in order to implement standardized weights and measures on schedule, instructed the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday: "In order to comply with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Industrial Character No. 4043, the Ministry presented to the government last year to convene representatives from various central ministries, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, and domestic experts to organize a Committee for the Promotion of Standardized Weights and Measures to formulate a unified national weights and measures procedure, stipulating that the sixteen provinces along the Yangtze River and the coast with convenient transportation, industrial and commercial economic development, as well as the capital, Shanghai, Beiping, Tianjin, Hankou, Qingdao, and Guangzhou, should complete standardization by the end of the 20th year of the Republic of China. The ten provinces of Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Yunnan, Guizhou, Sichuan, Xinjiang, and Xiamen should complete standardization by the end of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Tibet, Qinghai, and Xikang should complete standardization by the end of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. This procedure has already been submitted to the Executive Yuan for submission to the National Government for approval and filing, and has been distributed to the provincial and municipal governments for reference. Cases are on file. Currently, fourteen provinces and six cities have formulated procedures for standardized weights and measures and submitted them to the Ministry for verification and filing. Several other provinces have also submitted them and are being reviewed. In addition, due to frequent military uprisings, there has been no time to take care of standardization matters. Except for a few provinces and cities that can handle the case as is, many of those that have already handled it have also been restricted by military affairs and cannot actively proceed. Fortunately, the military suppression has been pacified and the overall situation has been settled, so the work should be stepped up in a timely manner to lay the foundation for the reorganization of national administration. For this reason, the Ministry specially held a National Weights and Measures Conference in November of this year to consult with various central agencies and provincial and municipal governments to select representatives, and to invite experts in the study of weights and measures to gather together to jointly discuss the new system promotion methods in the future. The Ministry, based on the national weights and measures unification procedures, drafted a plan requesting that the provincial and municipal governments unify on schedule, and submitted a proposal for discussion (this is the Ministry's first proposal for this conference), which is divided into four sections: First, training and testing personnel; second, establishing testing offices to implement administrative affairs; third, promoting manufacturing; and fourth, completing testing and inspection work. Each section is further divided into detailed items for explanation. After discussion and resolution by the conference, it was approved to be submitted for filing and distributed to the provincial and municipal governments for reference. Check the original case of the four sections listed, which are the key tasks for promoting the new system today, and should be organized without delay. However, the situations in the provinces and cities are inconsistent, so the steps taken in handling them are also very different. Now, the four sections of the original case are presented for printing, in addition to being submitted for filing, and distributed to the relevant departments, and a copy is enclosed, hoping that you will check the various regulations and methods of the national weights and measures unification procedure, and check which of the items listed in each section have been handled and which have not, determine the implementation plan, and proceed quickly so that it can be unified as scheduled, and submit the proposed plan to the Ministry for verification, which is truly beneficial to the public. etc. With this approval, the original method is copied and sent to the bureau, and you are required to comply with it and instruct it to be handled accordingly. This order."

The Ministry of Finance's Anti-Smuggling Office Will Move to Beijing Tomorrow 125

The Ministry of Finance's Anti-Smuggling Office on Manufacturing Bureau Road in this port has been ordered to move to Beijing. Yesterday, the office's documents, furniture, etc. were packed and transported. All office staff are scheduled to be led by Deputy Director Ke Sen to go to Beijing on the (18th). The Beijing address has been surveyed and is next to the Ministry of Finance at the Erlang Temple in the city. It is understood that the office originally had jurisdiction over thirteen anti-smuggling bureaus in the five prefectures of Jiangsu, Changlu, and Liangzhe, and four anti-smuggling special service regiments. Later, in order to reduce expenses, the Ministry of Finance abolished six agencies in Hubei, Hunan, Southern Anhui, Northern Anhui, Fujian, and Jiangxi. The existing ones are only seven bureaus in the five prefectures of Jiangsu, Liangzhe, Changlu, Huainan, Huaibei, Sichuan, and Northern Sichuan. Currently, the Special Service First Regiment is stationed in Huaibei, the Second Regiment is stationed in Jiujiang, and the Third and Fourth Regiments are stationed in Huainan. The original anti-smuggling teams on other coasts will all be given money and dismissed. As for the internal organization of the office, it was originally divided into five sections for handling affairs: General Affairs, Confidential Affairs, Management, Anti-Smuggling, and Medical Affairs. It is said that after moving to Beijing, it will also have to be reduced in size, and it is planned to abolish the Medical Affairs Section.

Central

The Achievements of Yangsi Cotton Farm Promotion 139

Farmers Gave Souvenirs Publicly

The Yangsi Cotton Crop Experiment Farm of the National Central University College of Agriculture is located in Yangsi District, Pudong, this city. Since its establishment, it has been more than ten years. In addition to focusing on Jiangyin white seed cotton breeding and cultivation method experiments, it also carries out promotion work. In recent years, it has made considerable achievements. Local cotton farmers are very enthusiastic about receiving cotton seeds from the farm and inquiring about cultivation methods. In order to carefully carry out the business, the farm has temporarily limited the promotion area to nearby villages and has not been able to popularize it elsewhere. This year, Chen Zixin, the Yangsi District City Committee, specially approved the Social Bureau for the purpose of improving and promoting cotton planting in the district, and donated funds to create ten cotton planting cooperative experiment farms in the district to serve as a demonstration and to promote the promotion. The cotton seeds used in all cooperative places and the technical guidance are all the responsibility of the farm. Now that the harvest season is over, Ma Shusheng District is the best, with an average yield of 162 catties per mu. The average yield of other districts is also more than 120 catties per mu, which is 20% more than that of farmers who use ordinary seeds and cultivate them in the old way. The farmers in each district are grateful for the quality of the farm's cotton seeds and the enthusiastic guidance of the promoters. They specially gave a silver district with the words "Agricultural Tutor" written on it to commemorate the occasion. Chen Zixin, the city committee member of the district, also compensated 120 yuan because the promoters of the farm provided voluntary guidance, ran around the fields in the hot summer, and obtained a bumper harvest. It is heard that the promoters of the farm took the guidance work as their duty and could not accept it without authorization. They asked the Dean of the College and instructed that the farm should be used in the name of the farm for cotton promotion in the district.

Local News 2

Two Bandits Sentenced to Death in the Huangpu River Smuggling and Murder Case 141

Yao Zucheng Sentenced to Two and a Half Years in Prison

Zhang Genbao, Feng Qing, and Yao Zucheng, the notorious bandits who robbed the Huangpu Small Steamboat of the Public Works Bureau of the Huangpu River and shot and killed Chinese and Western engineers, were escorted to the local court for adjudication. At 11:00 a.m. yesterday, Judge Wu Zhenkai pronounced the verdict in the Fifth Tribunal, ordering the defendants Zhang Genbao, Feng Qing, and Yao Zucheng to be brought before the court. The judge immediately stood up and recited the main text of the judgment: Zhang Genbao and Feng Qing were sentenced to death for joint robbery and murder, and deprived of their civil rights for life. Yao Zucheng was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment for receiving stolen goods and deprived of his civil rights for five years. The sentences imposed on Zhang Genbao and Feng Qing were based on the Law for the Punishment of Bandits, so the bailiffs were ordered to take them into custody immediately. Yao Zucheng was asked if he accepted the sentence, as he was sentenced for receiving 100 yuan of stolen goods. Yao still claimed that he was wronged and did not accept the sentence. The judge ordered him to appeal to the Jiangsu Higher Court within ten days after receiving the judgment and also ordered him to be returned to custody.

Ye Ziheng

The Family Has Many Storms 142

The Divorce Case Has Just Ended

A Lawsuit Has Arisen Between the Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law

The Female Lawyer Vigorously Mediates

Ye Paid a Huge Sum of Money to Have His Daughter-in-Law Separate

Gu Yaojuan, the daughter-in-law of Ye Ziheng, previously filed a lawsuit in the Civil Tribunal of the Special District Local Court, requesting to divorce her husband, Ye Kangnan. It has been peacefully settled through the mediation of relatives and friends. Recently, Ms. Gu hired a lawyer to sue her mother-in-law, Ye Zhang, in the Criminal Tribunal of the Special Court for embezzlement, etc. The reasons for her lawsuit are roughly as follows: "The plaintiff is the defendant's daughter-in-law, and all the wedding gifts and jewelry are managed by the plaintiff. However, the defendant, citing the unrest in the situation, instructed her to hand them over for safekeeping on her behalf. The plaintiff believed her to be true and handed them over completely. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff filed a divorce lawsuit this time, and then a settlement was reached. According to the terms of the settlement, all the wedding gifts and jewelry should be returned to the plaintiff. However, the defendant refused to hand them over, resulting in the return of only nine pieces of wedding gifts and jewelry. Among these nine pieces, five pieces were purchased temporarily from Yang Qinghe Silver Building on Nanjing Road and were not the original items, and the materials were very different from the original materials. The defendant initially claimed that the situation was unstable and asked the plaintiff to hand over the jewelry to her, and this time she hid the original items and temporarily purchased jewelry with very different materials, hoping to deceive her. The defendant used fraudulent means to implement embezzlement, which is very obvious and constitutes the crime of Article 363 and 356 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, please arrest her for questioning. However, the defendant is extremely cunning and may flee at any time. Please issue an arrest warrant as soon as possible. If the accusation is false, she is willing to sit in the crime of false accusation, etc." The court approved the words and signed an summons, ordering the arrest to be summoned to 105 Tongyi Lane, Jing'an Temple Road. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Cheng Shangfeng came to the court to open the trial. Neither the plaintiff nor the defendant turned themselves in. According to the complaint of the Chinese police, they were ordered to summon them with a court summons, but there was no number 105 on Tongyi Lane, so there was no way to deliver the summons, etc. The lawyer representing the plaintiff also rose to state the case and requested that the account books of Yang Qinghe Silver Building be checked so that it could be clarified. After verification by Judge Cheng, he instructed that the summons be reissued at a later date. It is also heard that this case has been mediated by a famous female lawyer and there is hope of a settlement. The condition is that the father, Ye Ziheng, paid a huge sum of money to have his daughter-in-law separate first. Yesterday, 100,000 yuan was handed over to a lawyer to have his daughter-in-law separate first, and it is expected to be resolved in a few days.

In the Safe

Embezzlement Case of 20,000 Yuan 143

Rong Xilin and Wang Jingqing Accused

Newly Installed Safe Unreliable

Rong Xilin of Rong Xiji Cotton Firm at 409 Zhoujin Lane, Hankou Road, from Wuxi, and his employed partner Wang Jingqing, are accused of stealing 20,000 silver dollars deposited by Zhu Jingan, the Shanghai-based manager of the Litai Textile Factory of Taicang, from Anhui province. Following Zhu’s accusation, the Special District Local Court, under Judge Ge, held a trial yesterday. According to the plaintiff, Rong had a contract with Litai to handle cotton transactions. Last month, the factory sent an employee, Gu Baotang, to Shanghai with 20,000 yuan in cash to purchase cotton locally. Rong Xilin invited Gu to stay at his firm and persuaded him to deposit the cash with him for safekeeping. However, on the second night, the defendant allegedly instructed his partner Wang Jingqing to secretly open the safe and steal the money. Gu Baotang testified that on the 17th of last month, he and his colleague Cao Sanduo came to Shanghai with 20,000 silver dollars to buy cotton in Datuantuan. They met the defendant, who invited them to stay at his firm, claiming that he had a newly installed safe suitable for storing money, ensuring that even if something went wrong, the funds would be safe. He even offered to entrust the keys to Gu. Lured by these sweet words, Gu placed all the money in the safe. At the time, Wang Sanduo, Wang Jingqing, Chen Yuntang, and others were present. That evening, Wang Jingqing invited them to see a movie and have dinner, but Gu declined. However, Wang insisted on taking him to the nearby Rixin Garden for a bath. While Gu was bathing, Wang excused himself and never returned. Upon returning to the defendant’s firm, Gu found that the safe was unlocked. Opening it, he discovered that all the silver dollars were gone, and Wang had also disappeared. Gu believed that there must have been two identical keys, one given to him for safekeeping, and the other remaining in the hands of the defendants, leaving no doubt about their guilt. Rong Xilin, the defendant, testified that Wang Jingqing was not his employed partner but was merely staying at his firm temporarily because he was unemployed. Gu Baotang had known Wang for a long time, and Gu voluntarily brought the money to be stored, having nothing to do with Rong. Judge Ge ordered Rong Xilin to post 20,000 yuan bail or a shop guarantee; lacking bail, Rong was detained and the hearing was adjourned.

Shanghai Municipal Sanitation Matters

Management Transferred to Public Security Bureau 145

The cleaning and sweeping of Shanghai Municipality, formerly under the jurisdiction of the Municipal Health Bureau, will now be managed by the Public Security Bureau, according to a recent decision by the Municipal Government to facilitate police command and supervision. Unprecedented Exchange in the Banking Sector 146

San Francisco Bank Executive Manager

Comes to Shanghai to Serve at Shanghai Bank

Wells Fargo Bank of San Francisco, recognizing the significant progress of the Chinese banking sector in recent years and its rising momentum, has reached an agreement with Chen Guangfu, General Manager of the Shanghai Bank, to send its Executive Manager, Mr. Wallis, to Shanghai to work as an employee of the Shanghai Bank, aiming to exchange knowledge and experience with the Chinese banking sector. Mr. Wallis has already arrived in Shanghai to fulfill his service of exchanging knowledge. While there are often examples of universities exchanging professors between countries (such as teachers from University A and University B agreeing to exchange positions for one or two years) to achieve an even progress in knowledge and experience, this is an unprecedented first in the banking sector. Wells Fargo Bank and Shanghai Bank have uniquely initiated this practice, which can be seen as a precursor to cooperation between Chinese and foreign banks. It is reported that the Shanghai Bank has not yet designated personnel to serve at Wells Fargo Bank, but outstanding bank staff will soon be selected and sent to the United States to implement the exchange of knowledge and experience.

Fishing Boat Sinks Freighter 150

Three Crew Members Drown

At 5:40 PM on the day before yesterday, a Jinbaoli freighter carrying yellow sand and gravel was entering Wusong from the Yangtze River estuary. While navigating through Zhanghuabang, a Yongmao fishing boat from the Nanshi Yongsheng Fishing Company suddenly sped towards it. Despite the freighter crew’s desperate attempts to steer clear, the Yongmao boat seemed to ignore them completely, not even sounding its horn, and rammed straight into the freighter. The freighter immediately capsized, and all eight crew members fell into the water. Hearing the loud cries for help, the Yongmao boat finally stopped its engine. Simultaneously, rescue boats from the Rescue Bureau and customs boats from the Wusong branch office rushed to the scene and began the rescue efforts. Five crew members were rescued, but the other three could not be reached, and their bodies were nowhere to be found. The drowned were identified as Wang Along, 31 years old, from Dinghai; Guan Atu, 25 years old, from Ningbo; and Hong Afa, 23 years old, from Dinghai. Following the accident, the Jianghai Customs investigated the vessel at fault to prepare a report. Upon hearing this tragic news, the families of the deceased wept and wailed, a truly heartbreaking scene. Shao Xubai and Wang Azeng, the owners of the freighter, have separately petitioned the Jianghai Customs Superintendent and the Wusong District Water Patrol of the Public Security Bureau, requesting that Yongsheng Company be held responsible for compensating the loss of the ship and cargo, and for providing generous compensation to the families of the deceased crew members. They have also sent letters to the Ningbo Fellow-Countrymen Association and other organizations, requesting assistance.

Tugboat Collides with Cotton Boat: The Shanghai Xieji Shenzhuang Cotton Firm hired a dock boat owned by Zhang Shungen the day before yesterday to transport 160 bales of cotton from the Pudong factory, heading north to the Suzhou River to deliver the cotton to the Yihe Yuan packing factory. The Yinping launch failed to avoid the coal boat, causing it to capsize and sink all the coal to the bottom of the river. Tap Water Pen Factory Hosts Banquet for All Sectors 155

Since its establishment as the first manufacturer of high-quality fountain pens in China, the Great China Tap Water Pen Factory has been in operation for two years. Because of the backwardness of our country’s industrial production, we still rely on foreigners for food and clothing. According to a recent survey, more than 600 million taels of silver are sent abroad each year for these two items. If something were to happen between China and foreign countries, they would stop supplying us with food and clothing before even attacking us, and some of us would starve immediately. Therefore, we must realize this early, rise up, and strive for industrial revolution. Zhang Zilian of the National Products Joint Market then spoke, stating that the first responsibility of a person in society is to fulfill their human duties, regardless of hardship and difficulty. If we can fulfill our human duties, success is not something to be overly happy about, and failure is not something to be ashamed of. For example, promoting national products is something that Chinese people should do, but some people are secretly jealous and destructive, showing that there are not many people in society who can truly be called human beings. Mr. Zhang's speech was poignant, and everyone in attendance was moved. The guests and hosts parted on good terms at around 9:00 PM.

Suppression of Flower Gambling in the Chinese Concession 156

Director Yuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recognizing the rampant gambling of flower gambling among citizens, despite repeated prohibitions, continues to be openly defied, causing great harm to the area. He issued a notice to all district offices last month, instructing them to pay close attention and giving patrol officers the temporary right to inspect pedestrians. Anyone found with flower gambling documents or evidence should be immediately arrested, pre-trialed, and then handed over to the bureau for punishment, without unauthorized disposition. Therefore, in recent days, the number of flower gambling cases detained in various district offices and transferred to the head office has decreased compared to last month. According to a staff member of the head office yesterday, if strict enforcement continues, it is expected that flower gambling in the Chinese Concession will come to an end in two months.

Russian Dancer

Fiance Injures Foot, Case Awaits Sentencing 157

The case of Russian woman Asia Tolo, 19 years old, being shot in the foot by her lover, Peter Lich, in a house at 104 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession last month has been previously reported. Now that the plaintiff has recovered, the police sent the defendant to the French Court for further investigation. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that it was unknown whether the shooting was caused by emotional turmoil or intentional harm. The lawyer found it incomprehensible that the plaintiff was only 19 years old, while the defendant was over 40, engaging in gambling at the General Assembly and seducing women, acting as a gigolo. The plaintiff was seduced by the defendant in Harbin when she was only 17 years old, under the pretext of no wife and considerable wealth, leading to her loss of virginity. Later, she found out that the defendant had a wife and several children, and when she confronted him, the defendant claimed to have divorced his wife. They then came to Shanghai together, living together as if they were married. The plaintiff behaved properly, but the defendant often went out and did not return, and had affairs. When she advised him, she was insulted and scolded. This spring, the defendant went to Hong Kong for several months, and upon returning to Shanghai, he abused the plaintiff even more, leading to their separation. The plaintiff had to work as a dancer at a dance hall to make a living. When the defendant found out, he often caused trouble at the dance hall, and finally shot and injured the plaintiff's foot, trying to prevent her from working as a dancer and cutting off her livelihood. According to a Western doctor, the plaintiff's leg has been permanently disabled, and the lawyer requested severe punishment and compensation of 10,000 yuan. The defendant, Peter Lich, also hired a lawyer to defend him, stating that he shot the plaintiff's leg due to mental stimulation and not intentional harm. He stated that the plaintiff seduced him first, and because of her affection, he abandoned his wife and children to come to Shanghai with her. On the day of the incident, both parties went to a tailor shop to order clothes and then went out. The plaintiff insisted on going to a Russian man named Feiteloff, but the defendant believed that this man was his enemy and tried to stop her in vain. The defendant was angry and fired a shot at the ground, intending to scare her, but unfortunately, the bullet bounced off the ground and injured the plaintiff's foot. The defendant used to serve the country on the battlefield, which caused his irritable nature. He was very remorseful afterwards and had no malicious intent, requesting leniency. As for the private prosecution, the plaintiff's injury was minor and there was no significant loss, requesting dismissal. The Chinese and Western officials concluded the debate and will await sentencing.

Key topics include: Reorganization of the Portion of Domestic Debt Bonds with and without Real Security (Part 2), The Relationship Between U.S. Reserves and the World Gold Problem (Part 1), Improvement Issues of Small Local Banks in the U.S. (Part 1), Research on No-Par Value Shares, Investigation of Jiang Kun's Financial Report, Report of the League of Nations World Gold Expert Committee (3), and a Comprehensive Overview of National Government Bonds, among other works.

News from the Jiangsu Provisional Charity Relief Association 167

The Jiangsu Provisional Charity Relief Association recently received a plea for relief from the Huaiyin Relief Association, stating that the county is an important town in northern Jiangsu. Due to the country's troubles, the suppression troops were few, and bandits rose from all directions, gathering into large groups, devastating the entire territory. Villages and towns were turned into ruins, countless people were captured, property was looted, and thousands of houses were burned, affecting tens of thousands of people. Faced with the chilling north wind, sleeping in the open and exposed to the elements, and crying out for food, the disaster is the worst in decades. The association has requested the provincial government to allocate 10,000 yuan and collect donations to send Zhou Yuankai and Li Yushu to investigate and provide urgent relief. It is also reported that Yancheng, Funing, Siyang, Suqian, and other counties have suffered severe banditry disasters, and their pleas for relief have also arrived in Shanghai, filled with tears and sorrow. The association has sent Commissioner Wang Yiting to the province to advocate for relief.

Jisheng Association Plans Emergency Relief for Jiangxi 168

The China Jisheng Association is currently providing disaster and industrial relief in Liaoning, Beiping, Shaanxi, Zhejiang, and Jiangsu, with hundreds of personnel working in the ice and snow, braving dangers. The internal staff are acting like Bao Xu weeping in the Qin court, begging for mercy from all the great philanthropists, restless day and night. They recently received a letter from the Jiangxi Ji'an Association in Shanghai, detailing the natural disasters followed by banditry in the area, causing extreme hardship, and requesting relief. Kindhearted comrades from the Shanghai Moral Association, with unbearable compassion, have initiated emergency relief for Ji'an and other places in Jiangxi, inviting the association to join. The association, burdened with numerous relief efforts and limited funds, has put it to a general assembly for a decision, hoping to contribute what it can and support the righteous cause. They hope that compassionate and benevolent individuals from all walks of life will generously offer a little to benefit the disaster victims.

Due to repeated refusals from members, it was impossible to raise funds. On the spot, the committee members reluctantly recognized 500 yuan to fulfill their national obligations; (4) Wang Xietai requested the association to help recover the outstanding payments from the workers of the shop and discuss the freedom to suspend business and seek new employment. Resolved: First, send Chen Yunhe to investigate and then make a decision; (5) Distribute calendars to all members to strengthen member relations and promote the national calendar. Resolved: Proceed as planned; the rest is omitted.

Western Dye Industry: The Western Dye Industry Association sent a letter yesterday to the representatives Li Shiyan, Wang Zuolin, Shen Yaoshan, and Zhang Zhenhou of the consolidated industry regarding Guanghua Dye Company's excuse for delaying membership due to its concurrent engagement in dyeing and weaving, stating: "Dear Sirs, Regarding the Guanghua Dye Company's case of delaying membership due to its concurrent engagement in the dyeing and weaving industry, we have received a letter from the factory stating that it has decided to withdraw. Our association has already sent a reply, which briefly states: 'We have received your letter stating that our dye business has been declining in recent years, and we have decided to specialize in dyeing and weaving and have joined the Machine-Made National Products Association, and we are withdrawing from your association. Upon investigation, your company was already listed as a Western dye industry member before the Shanghai Foreign Goods Nine Industries Association, affiliated with the Western Dye Industry, was abolished. It is a narrow and complete group. Our association has been handling the aforementioned consolidation for several months, and the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau have repeatedly ordered compliance. Furthermore, at the mediation convened by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the 21st of last month, the first item was: (1) Gonghe Lai and other sixteen companies should join the Western Dye Industry Association to strengthen unity and must join before the end of November, etc., which has been reported to the higher authorities for record. Gonghe et al. have already submitted their applications to join the association in compliance with the order. Since your company's joining our association is within the scope of determined consolidation, you should fulfill the obligation to join without any delay or excuse that can be changed. Moreover, tracing back, your company has always regarded the Western dye industry as the basic business entity, which goes without saying. Even if your letter claims to be engaged in the dyeing and weaving industry concurrently, you should also join the respective industry associations separately in accordance with the law in order to comply with the legal system. In this case, no matter how much the Western dye business of your company declines, it is a disguise to resist and quibble. In short, your company holds dissenting opinions, which are close to disobeying the orders of the higher authorities, which is inappropriate. Therefore, we urgently reject your appeal and hope that your company will investigate and promptly contact our association's consolidation committee members Li Shiyan and Wang Zuolin to obtain the application form, fill it out, and submit it to our association for verification and transfer. Please do not wait and see and miss the opportunity. This is very important.' Upon investigation, the factory is one of the sixteen companies that the higher authorities mediated and consolidated. In fact, legally and commercially, there is an extreme need to fulfill the obligation, and there is no room for debate or avoidance. The matter concerns mediation on record, and we hereby request you to investigate accordingly. Gentlemen, you are responsible for the whole group of sixteen companies and have the full authority to handle the consolidation. Please provide a sincere and thorough explanation and submit the application form to our association as soon as possible to complete the procedures and determine the unity, and please inform us of the progress of the handling as soon as possible so that we can handle it. We are extremely looking forward to it, etc."

Weather Report 177

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday, stating: The weather in the Yangtze River basin and the coastal areas here is cloudy and changeable, and there is a risk of rain and fog due to the low pressure in central China. The wind along the coast and in the Yangtze River basin is gentle and non-directional. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 48.0 and the lowest was 43.2.

Letter 178

Dear Editor, I recently read in your newspaper's local news section the section on Zheng Xiangqian's dangerous injuries, which stated that Zheng Xiangqian, who runs the Yucheng Doumai Firm, also runs the Jiuchongtian Club in Taiyuanfang in the French Concession. I was deeply shocked. The so-called Zheng Xiangqian is a distant cousin of the owner of our firm. He used to work in our firm but left due to some matters and has been making a living on his own for several years. He has nothing to do with our firm. What your newspaper reported is a difference of a thousand miles. It must be a rumor. I hereby ask you to correct it and publish it in the letter section to clarify the truth. Thank you very much. Sincerely, Shanghai Yucheng Shushu, December 16.

Green Garden

The Bud Society of the People's Livelihood Middle School 180

Wouldn't this count as a miracle? That in such a barren, desolate world there would be such a lovely bud produced. But the facts tell us that it certainly is. The Bud Society has been organized at the People's Livelihood Middle School, and it is expected to have a permanent life.

To put it simply, there are several young people still at the People's Livelihood Middle School who have a sense of national consciousness and are enthusiastically willing to work, struggle, advance, and sacrifice for our own art, and to establish a new life for art. Therefore, they have organized a small group to irrigate it with a spirit and power of cooperation, so that this nascent bud will gradually flourish and grow.

They are divided into drama, music, art, and literature departments, which shows that their organization is complete and their purpose is pure. It is definitely not like the general blind youth societies of the time, which have neither clear doctrine nor understanding, and even less content and reality.

In short, the Bud Society, as its name gives us the image, is still a lovely flower bud that is about to bloom. The flowers that will bloom in the future will surely be very beautiful and vibrant. Moreover, it also symbolizes the greatness of the eve of the great era of the future.

Quarterly Journal of the Class of 1920 of the Law Department is About to be Published 182

The open road of the times is safely laid out before our eyes. The revolutionary vigor fills the whole country. The general trend of youth literary works is like a rising wind and surging clouds. This is indeed a good phenomenon in China's academic circles, worthy of admiration and dancing.

Of course, the literary groups in various universities are the ones who promote the brilliance of the academic world. Generally, young students with creative desires are unwilling to bury their talents, so in their spare time, they are organizing various societies and associations like rain after spring shoots to express their new spirit of life.

Since the Shanghai Second Academy of Culture started this semester, the school has been striving to improve. The new campus has been purchased at Wenzhi Road, Jiangwan. It is said that bids for the construction of its large-scale Western-style building will be invited soon. All professors in various departments are scholars with specialized research at home and abroad, so the progress of students' achievements is improving day by day, almost by leaps and bounds. In recent months, the general students have spared no effort in promoting the new culture and are full of energy. The rise of those literary groups is really colorful and varied, all showing amazing brilliance. The most trusted and praised by the students is the Class of 1920 of the Law Department. Among them, enthusiastic and responsible members such as Sun Zhide, Li Jiarong, Lai Jian, and Li Yuyue are willing to sacrifice for the association affairs, and they all show a gentle and friendly attitude towards the students, which is indeed worthy of the students' trust and admiration. It is now heard that the association is publishing a quarterly journal. Since the solicitation of manuscripts, students have been enthusiastically contributing. The content is divided into essays, current affairs reviews, and literary works. The materials are abundant, which goes without saying. In particular, there are the most works on the exploration of social sciences, the interpretation of legal principles, and national consciousness. The entire length is as much as 200,000 words, which is truly a huge publication in Shanghai's student circles. It is now actively being printed and will be published in the near future. It is also heard that it has been agreed with a certain bookstore to be its agent.

Green Garden

Wang Tiehua After the Law School Was Registered 183

Since the Ministry of Education approved the establishment of the Shanghai Law School on the 4th of this month, the news spread and the whole school rejoiced. Immediately, more than 700 students and faculty gathered in the large first classroom (the auditorium is about to begin construction) to hold a temporary general meeting. It was decided that all faculty, staff, and students would go to the North Railway Station to welcome Provost Shen, who had been working hard in Beijing awaiting orders. Although there was no definite knowledge of which train Provost Shen would return on, everyone, unable to contain their enthusiasm, immediately hired a long line of cars, waved flags, and shouted, heading straight to the North Station from Jiangwan Road.

Express trains and fast trains all arrived, but our handsome Provost Shen was nowhere to be seen. We were not disappointed; we still returned to school in a grand and orderly fashion, because other work was waiting for us to carry out.

The sunlight after the rain was shining on our school, making it feel exceptionally bright and warm, like the arrival of new life. The sunlight shone brightly on the five characters of our "Shanghai Law School" plaque.

The students of the whole school were wildly joyful, and slogans were posted all over the school. Clever sayings poured out like a string of pearls. The Anhui Provincial Association hung a banner at the school gate with the large characters "Continue the Efforts After Registration." Upon entering through the main gate, both sides of the path were filled with slogans from various grade associations, provincial associations, and academic societies, full of praise and blessings, both serious and humorous. Some examples include: "Celebrate the Success of Registration," "Support the Dedicated Educators President Chu and Provost Shen," "Although Registration Has Succeeded, Students Must Work Harder," "Registration is the Result of Effort, but Also the Beginning of a New Start," "Create the Highest Academic Institution in the East, Which Should Be the Goal After Registration." The most interesting ones boldly proclaimed, "Welcome Provost Shen, Who Has Contributed Greatly," and "Welcome Provost Shen's Triumphant Return." Mr. Shen was working tirelessly on the Jing-Hu Road (Beijing-Shanghai Railway) for the school's registration, submitting the final designs and plans for the auditorium and library. Therefore, the news of the registration's approval reached the school through Mr. Shen's telegram. The students did not hesitate to go to the station to welcome Mr. Shen, which shows their love for the school and their deep respect for Mr. Shen.

Amidst the school-wide celebration, the members of the "Law Research Association," who always lead the elite, became even busier. While rushing to complete a 300,000-word "Law Journal," they had to take the time to express their enthusiastic congratulations. Under the clock tower in the classroom, they hung a large banner with the large characters "Celebrate the Success of Registration" written in beautiful and eye-catching fonts. On either side were couplets more than ten feet long, which read:

"The whole school rejoices, seeing today smiles blooming, slogans flying like butterflies, banners dancing like dragons, it is the beginning of a new life. Come, come, let us all shout 'Long live the Law School!' We should encourage each other, remembering the hard work of the past, the foundation firmly established, the reputation soaring like an eagle, wanting to realize a grand plan. Forward, forward, dare to encourage our comrades to avoid one day's heat and ten days' cold."

Our Mr. Shen, on the second day, in the smiling sun and the embrace of the train, smilingly walked slowly out of the station. After a brief delay at home, he hastily arrived at the school. President Chu also came. The whole school was filled with excitement. The chairmen and committee members of various class associations were busy holding meetings to discuss how to celebrate. Slogans, like butterflies, were constantly pasted all over the school, piled on top of each other, attracting students from neighboring schools to come and visit. The Songhu (Shanghai-Hangzhou) trains constantly passed by the school gate, almost causing the passengers to crane their necks out of the carriages. The enthusiasm was truly indescribable, beyond the ability of my clumsy pen to describe.

The school authorities were naturally as happy as the students. Knowing that the students were eager to see the provost, they did not wait for the memorial week next Monday but held a general meeting on this Saturday afternoon, where Provost Shen reported on the process.

Amidst the welcoming cheers of more than 1,500 hands, Mr. Shen took the stage with a voice filled with emotion. A ray of sunlight was shining in from the west window, and a gentle breeze was blowing his beautiful beard. He couldn't help but smile. His speech was slightly trembling. At this moment, Mr. Shen was experiencing indescribable joy.

He first described the school's efforts and the process of applying for registration over the years, with witty remarks that excited the whole audience. When he talked about registration being like a man proposing to a woman, the female students laughed uncontrollably. Mr. Shen stood tall on the stage, his demeanor no less than when he was a groom in his younger days. He said that the success of registration was like a man getting a woman's consent to his proposal and being able to get married, equally joyful, but marriage is a person's joy, while the success of registration is the joy of all the faculty and students. Finally, he encouraged the students to work harder in the future and guaranteed that next year's graduates would be able to hold the ceremony in the new auditorium, and at the same time, there would be a 100,000-yuan fundraising to build a large library and purchase a large number of books.

There are only two weeks left before the summer vacation. To celebrate and commemorate, we will hold a ceremony for the completion of the school building and the laying of the foundation stone for the grand auditorium on Friday and Saturday of next week, as well as a grand entertainment fair. At that time, we will, of course, invite guests to come and give us their guidance.

Writing to this point, a sense of joy and celebration spontaneously rushes to my fingertips. My heart is beating passionately, and my hand is trembling so much that I can no longer write. However, I would like to excerpt a few sentences from a declaration by the Class of 1931 Association to conclude this article:

"Our school was established in the 15th year of the Republic of China (1926) and has experienced many ups and downs. Fortunately, danger could be turned into safety... President Chu came to lead our school, and Mr. Shen assisted him... In no time, it transformed from a law college with nothing to a law school with a solid foundation... It is heard that the Ministry of Education approved the registration a few days ago. Upon hearing this, the whole school went wild. In this cheering, we still hope that the two gentlemen will actively plan the development of the school, aiming to rival Oxford University, to wash away the shame of backwardness in Eastern education... It is believed that the day of registration is the time to start, to build on the past and usher in the future, relying on the two gentlemen. Zhuangzi said, 'Its beginning is simple, its end will be great.' Applying this to our school, it is very close..."

Submission Guidelines for Youth Garden 184

(1) Articles should be about discussions on youth issues, news about domestic and foreign students or student affairs, essays, and descriptions of school life. The style is not limited.

(2) Illustrations should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photos should be of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, plays, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individual and group photos are welcome.

Market News 185

The Asia-America Company at 323 Jiangxi Road, Shanghai, declares that this company is the oldest business in China's radio industry and has been particularly strong in promoting radio in China. Now, this company will broadcast a special program on the evening of December 31st of this year. To promote interest in the national calendar, starting at 0:01 on January 1st, free New Year greetings will be broadcasted by radio telephone. Anyone who wants to use radio telephone to send New Year greetings only needs to fill in the names and addresses of the sender and receiver on the back of this company's invoice and mark the envelope "Asia-America Company Advertising Department." Those received before December 31st will be broadcast for free. This company will be closed from January 1st to 4th, 2021, and will resume business as usual on the 5th.

The Central Suitcase Factory on Jing'an Temple Road declares that this factory has been in business for more than ten years, and its products, such as leather suitcases, iron suitcases, and white boxes and layered board boxes, are all sturdy and perfect. Recently, to expand its business, this factory has specially established a distribution office at 76 Jing'an Temple Road. During this month, all customers will be sold at wholesale prices to show preferential treatment. Recently, the doors have been crowded, and there is a great rush to meet the demand.

The purpose is to promote China's sports and cultivate the nation's athletic spirit. The method is extraordinary, and the interest is particularly strong. The novelty of the style and the splendor and beauty of the decoration are secondary matters. The price is low, only four jiao (cents) per set. The Commercial Press and various bookstores in this port have distributors.

The Daguang Firm at 9 Hankou Road declares that the self-copying machine recently invented by Song Zijiang, the manager of this firm, is easy to use, prints clearly, and is beautifully decorated. The price is low, specially divided into three sizes: large, medium, and small. The large size is fifteen yuan, the medium size is eight yuan, and the small size is four yuan. The carefully made ink is sold in bottles. Currently, various commercial and municipal government agencies, associations, lawyers, and accountants in this port and other ports have been happy to use it. Now, to facilitate users, the management department is specially located at the Chinese Typewriter Company at 300 Jiangxi Road, and the two major bookstores in this port, Datong and Kaiming, are both acting as distributors.

The Lihua Company on Nanjing Road declares that the music department on the third floor of this company has newly arrived a large number of fourth-period Columbia Cantonese opera records, such as Bai Juyi and Rong Sao Yun's "Marriage Stone," Xue Juexian and Tang Xueqing's duet "Military Uniforms Deliver Poetry," Bai Juyi and Xiao Lizhang's duet "Red Boy," Lü Wencheng and Da Sha's "Late Year Fried Tweezers," Xiao Lizhang's "Wonderful Desert Counts Moon Pieces," and Xiang Wen's "Bao Dai Pities Fragrance," etc. All are masterpieces of famous actors, and there are many new records of various famous actors. During the discount period, all prices are reduced.

The Zhongmei Xiang Embroidery Shop at the west end of Zhoujin Lane, Sanma Road, declares that the various embroideries produced by this shop have always been famous. Many Chinese people love them, and foreigners love them even more. Automotive News Special Article

Match King Fortune Person 186

Reunion with Happy Owner

Mr. Krenger is a well-known European economist and industrialist. He recently traveled to the United States and visited his old friend Mr. C. W. Nash at the Nash Motors factory in Kenosha. The reunion of old friends was unspeakably joyful. In 1928, Mr. Nash had visited Stockholm, Sweden, and stayed for four days, receiving very hospitable treatment from Mr. Krenger. This was their first meeting.

Mr. Krenger is the globally renowned Match King. Mr. Nash is the world-admired automotive giant. The two have similar aspirations and are very close. In the beginning, they had no capital or power. However, they were able to endure hardship and hard work, which led to their great achievements today. One of these two is a mechanic, and the other is a transporter.

Both Mr. Krenger and Mr. Nash are major shareholders of the Lee Higginson Bank. Mr. Krenger's mission to the United States this time was to attend the opening ceremony of the Chicago branch of the Lee Higginson Bank. He took the opportunity to visit his old friend at his residence and also tour the famous scenic spots of the western United States.

In 1893, the World's Fair was held in Chicago, USA. Mr. Krenger went to the United States to seek a job. At first, he bought and sold real estate for others, earning a small commission. After accumulating fifty dollars, he left the United States and crossed the ocean. Today, Mr. Krenger is revisiting Chicago. The situation is very different, and he must have infinite feelings. And Mr. Krenger's situation is also very different.

This time, the Match King's visit to the United States was very welcomed by all sectors. The Chicago Industrial Association held a special banquet to entertain him. Mr. Krenger gave a speech on his views on solving the problem of repaying international public debt. His opinions were profound, and his words were long. Mr. Krenger is very familiar with debt matters and has rich experience. Therefore, Mr. Krenger is not only the Match King but also a debt expert.

It is found that the Swedish Match Factory supplies matches for 600 million people worldwide every day. It controls the match business in Europe, Asia, and South America and has exclusive sales rights. Mr. Krenger's ability to absorb world finance can only be rivaled by one or two people. The Swedish government's treasury relies on the factory's taxes, which are about ten million gold or more each year.

During Mr. Krenger's visit to the Nash Motors factory, he greatly praised the mechanical capabilities, movement styles, and equipment engineering of the new Nash Motors and was extremely satisfied. It is said that Nash Motors are as popular in Europe as they are in the Americas.

Left: Mr. Krenger Right: Mr. Nash

Discussion

Automotive Manufacturing Plant Construction Plan Wufi 187

In the past ten years, for the construction of highways, driving cars, national figures, have not been that the only construction in terms of developing transportation. As the road is opened, the automotive industry also followed it. In the backward of scientific our country, the only one item is purchased from the ship. Although the road construction in our country is more and more developed, it turns to more market for selling automotives for Euroupe and America. I don’t know how many profits were seized. That is one. Namely our country's major cities, have a so-called automotive company, whose above is merely to install various components into a car, and below is only to repair parts, configure tires only. If you say you can set up a factory to manufacture national automotive products, it is like a phoenix feather. That is two. Therefore, I think repairing roads, convenient transportation, is a current important issue. Manufacturing automotive products, is a strategies to recover profits. I had similar discuss and publish on last year. Recently "Construction Commission Working Plan Outline", for the construction plan of automotive manufacturing plan, its development process is divided into four phase of working plans. The plan is very detailed, so let's copy the full text as left, so that automotive workers and consumers will know.

National economy and people's livelihood are called traffic, the total reason is to promote in the shortest period, complete one million miles of road. At the same time, set up factories in appropriate places to manufacture automobiles, in order to transport and benefit the people's journey. Now the completed national highway is no less than 20,000 miles. Acting of the last training, quite efforts. The only the problem of automotive manufacturing is still not planned and held, which leads to daily vehicles, relying on foreign countries. Unfortunately. It found that the total amount of automotive imported in 18th year of the Republic of China(1929) was more than 3,600 vehicles. The value is more than 10 million, so the big of missing can be seen.

At this time of national unity, construction is the beginning, all business is bound to prosper. And the tools of action are also increasingly urgent. This Association inspects the trend of transportation development in other countries, and examines the daily needs of the people. Intending to follow President Sun Yat-Sen's will and in the shortest period, set up factories in Shanghai or other convenient transportation places, and manufacture automotive and similar action tools. From a small scale, specialized in manufacturing relatively simple commercial automobiles, i.e. long-distance automotive and transport vehicles, and training specialized workers talent. Second, gradually expand equipment, increase product types and production. First with set and copy. Continue to plan, test and manufacture new vehicles. Make sure the vehicles are suitable for our country's road conditions, and the raw materials used are mainly obtained from the country. In the future, all the vehicles needed in the country, small gasoline boats, and airplanes, etc., can be manufactured by the plant. If so, it can recover profits to the outside world and promote industry and commerce to the inside. National economy and people's livelihood, real benefits rely on. The construction and development process of the automotive manufacturing plant is divided into four phases. Each phase is three years. The main work of each phase is outlined below.

The first phase is the entrepreneurial period. The main work in this period should be temporarily limited to assembling foreign components and manufacturing commercial automotive body, frame, springs, and other simple parts. It can also be gradually copied. In the early years, one car can be produced per day. After the workers' skills are improved, it can be increased to three vehicles per day. The equipment must include a factory site, assembly plant, woodworking plant, metalworking plant, forging plant, painting plant, engine test room, office, drawing room, garage, warehouse, power engine, air compressor, woodworking machine, metalworking machine, forging machine, and corresponding hand tools, etc. All machinery and tools must be temporarily simple and able to manufacture the above-mentioned goods. However, the scale of the factory site and factory buildings must be relatively large in order to develop in the future. The initial capital required is approximately 800,000 yuan. Later, increase by 400,000 yuan each year. The total investment for the entire period is 1.6 million yuan.

The second phase is the imitation phase. In addition to continuing the work of the first phase and increasing the output, the important parts of automotive products should be imitated, such as transmission mechanisms. Walking mechanism. Starting mechanism and the body of the recreational automotive, etc. The output can be increased year by year according to the previous method. By the end of this period, five commercial vehicles, five recreational vehicles, and two agricultural vehicles must be produced every day. The equipment must include the expansion of all the equipment in the first phase, and the addition of a recreational automotive body manufacturing plant and the machinery required by the two plants. The capital increases by an average of 800,000 yuan each year. The total capital increase for the entire period is 2.4 million yuan.

The third phase is the design and manufacturing phase. In addition to continuing the work of the previous phase, the main parts of the entire automotive must be designed, tested, and manufactured by itself. The output can also be increased year by year according to the previous method. To the extent that it can produce ten commercial vehicles, one recreational vehicle, five agricultural vehicles, five motorcycles, and two electric vehicles per day. The equipment must include the expansion of all the equipment in the previous phase, and the addition of a test room and test equipment. The capital increases by an average of 2 million yuan each year. The total capital increase for the entire period is 6 million yuan.

The fourth phase is the expansion phase. In addition to continuing the work in phases, the business can be expanded as much as possible and the types and quantities of vehicles can be increased. At the same time, plan and manufacture small gasoline boats. Military vehicles. and aircraft. By the end of this period. Manufacturing capacity. Must reach the limit of 20 commercial vehicles per day. Forty recreational vehicles. Ten agricultural vehicles. Ten motorcycles. Five electric vehicles. and ten military vehicles per month. Five small gasoline boats. Five aircraft. The equipment must include the expansion of all the equipment in the previous phase. A shipyard should be added. Aircraft factory. and the machinery required by the two plants. The capital increases by an average of 4 million yuan each year. The total increase for the entire period is 12 million yuan. The total capital for the above four phases is 22 million yuan.
